代码里其实已经写了苹果毛玻璃风格：深色渐变背景、backdrop-blur、白色半透明卡片等。但用户截图显示的是「纯白背景+黑字、无样式」——说明很可能是：

我需要：
1. 在 layout.tsx 里加上 `import './globals.css'`
2. 给 body 加上背景等基础样式，确保即使 Tailwind 有问题也有底色
3. 确认 tailwind content 能扫到 app 下所有文件（已经包含 ./app/**）

另外看 page 里用的是 Tailwind 的 utility class，如 `min-h-screen`、`bg-gradient-to-br` 等，这些都依赖 Tailwind 编译。所以关键是让 globals.css 被引入。

Next.js 13+ App Router 约定：在 app/layout.tsx 里 import 的 globals.css 会自动全局生效，但必须有一行 import。当前 layout 没有任何 import，所以没有样式。

我加上 `import './globals.css'`，并给 body 一个默认背景色（作为 fallback），再强化一下 globals.css 里的玻璃效果和字体，确保苹果猫玻璃风格完整呈现。

assistant:
<think>
There's no postcss.config.js in the frontend root. Next.js 15 with Tailwind - when you install tailwindcss, you typically need a postcss.config.js that has tailwind and autoprefixer. Let me check Next.js 15 docs - actually Next.js can use tailwind without postcss.config if they're using the right setup. Let me read the tailwind docs - in Next.js 13+, you often have postcss.config.js with:
  plugins: {
    tailwindcss: {},
    autoprefixer: {},
  }
Without it, Tailwind might not be processed. So the issue could be:
1. Missing import of globals.css in layout (fixed)
2. Missing postcss.config.js - so Tailwind directives might not be compiled

I'll add postcss.config.js to be safe, and enhance globals.css with more explicit glass utilities and a base background so that even if Tailwind has any issue, we have fallbacks.
</think>
正在添加 PostCSS 配置并强化玻璃样式，确保 Tailwind 能正确编译。

const config = {

  },
}

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/3、自营项目/上帝之眼/frontend/app/components/BottomNav.tsx
  contents: /**
 * 底部导航 - 移动端毛玻璃 Tab 栏，适配安全区
 */
'use client'

import Link from 'next/link'
import { usePathname } from 'next/navigation'

const tabs = [
  { href: '/', label: '首页', icon: '🎯' },
  { href: '/signals', label: '信号', icon: '📡' },
  { href: '/experts', label: '高手', icon: '👥' },
  { href: '/stocks', label: '股票', icon: '📈' },
  { href: '/settings', label: '我的', icon: '⚙️' },
]

export default function BottomNav() {
  const pathname = usePathname()

  return (
    <nav
      className="fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 z-50 backdrop-blur-xl bg-white/10 border-t border-white/20 safe-area-bottom"
      style={{ paddingBottom: 'env(safe-area-inset-bottom, 0)' }}
    >
      <div className="flex items-center justify-around h-14 max-w-lg mx-auto">
        {tabs.map(({ href, label, icon }) => {
          const isActive = pathname === href || (href !== '/' && pathname.startsWith(href))
          return (
            <Link
              key={href}
              href={href}
              className={`flex flex-col items-center justify-center flex-1 py-2 min-w-0 transition-colors ${
                isActive ? 'text-white' : 'text-white/60'
              }`}
            >
              <span className="text-xl leading-none mb-0.5">{icon}</span>

        <div className="px-4 py-3">
          <h1 className="text-lg font-bold text-white">📈 股票监控</h1>
        </div>
      </header>

      <div className="px-4 py-4 space-y-3">
        {stocks.map((stock: any) => (
          <div
            key={stock.code}
            className="backdrop-blur-xl bg-white/10 border border-white/20 rounded-xl p-4 flex items-center justify-between"
          >
            <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
              <h3 className="font-bold text-white truncate">{stock.name}</h3>
              <p className="text-white/60 text-sm">{stock.code}</p>
              <p className="text-white/50 text-xs mt-1">{stock.sector}</p>
            </div>
            <div className="text-right flex-shrink-0 ml-3">
              <div className="text-lg font-bold text-white">¥{stock.price?.toFixed(2)}</div>
              <div
                className={`text-sm font-medium ${
                  stock.change_pct > 0 ? 'text-red-400' : 'text-green-400'
                }`}
              >
                {stock.change_pct > 0 ? '+' : ''}{(stock.change_pct * 100).toFixed(2)}%
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

蚂蚁财富 (Ant Fortune) typically uses:
- Primary: green/teal for positive/wealth (涨、收益) - like #00C087 or similar
- Red for rise (A-shares convention: 红涨绿跌 in China actually 红涨绿跌 - so red up green down in Chinese market)
- Actually in China stock: 红涨绿跌 (red = up, green = down), so many Chinese finance apps use red as primary for "up"
- Ant Fortune / 支付宝理财 often uses: deep blue/navy background, green for profit/positive, red for negative, gold/yellow for highlights, clean white cards

- Background: soft dark blue-gray (like iOS Control Center) or lighter gradient - 蚂蚁财富 often has a warmer dark or light theme. I'll go with a softer dark base with subtle blue/green tint (finance feel).

已按「苹果毛玻璃 + 蚂蚁财富」风格做完配色和布局统一，并丰富了「我的」页面。修改总结如下：

---

**1. 设计令牌（苹果毛玻璃 + 蚂蚁财富配色）**

- **`globals.css`** 增加 CSS 变量：
  - **背景**：深蓝灰渐变（`#0f1419` → `#1a2332`），类似苹果 Control Center。
  - **玻璃**：`rgba(255,255,255,0.08)` / `0.12`，细边框，统一毛玻璃感。
  - **蚂蚁财富风格**：涨 `#ff4d4f`、跌 `#00b96b`、主色支付宝蓝 `#1677ff`、高亮金 `#faad14`、辅助绿 `#00c087`。
- **`tailwind.config.js`** 扩展 `colors.godeye`：`up / down / primary / gold / green`，全站用 `text-godeye-up`、`bg-godeye-primary/30` 等统一风格。
- 涨跌语义：**A 股习惯红涨绿跌**，涨用红、跌用绿，与蚂蚁财富一致。

---

**2. 「我的」页面内容增强**

- **顶部**：头像、昵称（卡若）、ID；总资产（可隐藏）、今日收益；「明细」入口。
- **我的持仓（我买的股票）**：列表展示名称、代码、现价、盈亏与盈亏比例（红/绿）；「全部」跳转股票页。
- **自选股**：名称、代码、现价、涨跌幅；「管理」跳转股票页。
- **账户与设置**：订单记录、消息通知、帮助与反馈、关于上帝之眼（入口链接保留，子页可后续再做）。

当前「我的」为前端模拟数据；接入真实资产/持仓/自选股 API 后，只需替换数据源即可。

---

**3. 全站风格统一**

- **首页**：顶栏、视频区、三宫格、最新信号、核心策略均改为 `glass-card` / `glass-card-strong`，强调色用 `godeye-up/down/primary/gold/green`。
- **信号 / 高手 / 股票**：顶栏统一毛玻璃，列表与按钮统一新配色；信号「买入」、高手「关注」用支付宝蓝系；股票涨跌用红/绿。
- **底部导航**：使用 `glass-card-strong`，与顶栏一致。

---

**4. 使用方式**

- 开发环境：`cd frontend && npm run dev`，访问 `http://localhost:3000`。
- 「我的」在底部 Tab「我的」进入，可查看资产概览、持仓、自选股和设置入口。
- 子页如「订单记录」「关于」等链接已预留，后续在 `app/settings/` 下加对应路由即可。

若你希望某一块再偏蚂蚁财富一点（例如卡片圆角、间距、或某页单独配色），可以说具体页面或模块，我可以按页再细调一版。

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/3、自营项目/上帝之眼/backend/app/api/v1/me.py
  contents: """
我的 - 持仓、自选股、账户绑定、自动化交易 动态管理 API

- 自选股: 增删改查
- 我的持仓: 查询（可对接券商或本地）
- 交易账户: 绑定/选择/设为默认
- 自动化交易: 开关、策略选择、关联账户、风控参数
"""
from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException
from pydantic import BaseModel
from typing import List, Optional
from core.database import get_db

router = APIRouter(prefix="/me", tags=["我的"])

# 当前用户ID（后续可改为 JWT 解析）
def _user_id() -> str:
    return "user_001"


# ---------- 自选股 ----------
class WatchlistItem(BaseModel):
    code: str
    name: str

class WatchlistAdd(BaseModel):
    code: str
    name: str

@router.get("/watchlist")
async def get_watchlist():
    """获取自选股列表"""
    db = get_db()
    doc = await db.user_watchlist.find_one({"user_id": _user_id()})
    items = (doc or {}).get("items", [])
    # 兼容旧接口：若无则返回默认两条
    if not items:
        items = [{"code": "600519", "name": "贵州茅台"}, {"code": "000858", "name": "五粮液"}]
    return {"code": 200, "message": "success", "data": items}

@router.post("/watchlist")
async def add_watchlist(body: WatchlistAdd):
    """添加自选股"""
    db = get_db()
    await db.user_watchlist.update_one(
        {"user_id": _user_id()},
        {"$addToSet": "items", "$set": {"user_id": _user_id()}},
        upsert=True
    )
    # 正确用法：addToSet 要传对象
    await db.user_watchlist.update_one(
        {"user_id": _user_id()},
        {"$addToSet": {"items": {"code": body.code, "name": body.name}}, "$set": {"user_id": _user_id()}},
        upsert=True
    )
    return {"code": 200, "message": "已添加", "data": {"code": body.code, "name": body.name}}

@router.delete("/watchlist/{code}")
async def remove_watchlist(code: str):
    """删除自选股"""
    db = get_db()
    r = await db.user_watchlist.update_one(
        {"user_id": _user_id()},
        {"$pull": {"items": {"code": code}}}
    )
    if r.modified_count == 0 and r.matched_count == 0:
        await db.user_watchlist.update_one(
            {"user_id": _user_id()},
            {"$set": {"user_id": _user_id(), "items": []}},
            upsert=True
        )
    return {"code": 200, "message": "已移除", "data": {"code": code}}


# ---------- 我的持仓（买的股票）----------
@router.get("/holdings")
async def get_holdings():
    """获取我的持仓 - 可后续对接券商接口"""
    db = get_db()
    doc = await db.user_holdings.find_one({"user_id": _user_id()})
    items = (doc or {}).get("items", [])
    if not items:
        # 默认示例数据
        items = [
            {"name": "贵州茅台", "code": "600519", "cost": 1680, "current": 1720, "amount": 100, "pnl": 4000, "pnl_pct": 2.38},
            {"name": "宁德时代", "code": "300750", "cost": 198, "current": 205, "amount": 500, "pnl": 3500, "pnl_pct": 3.54},
            {"name": "招商银行", "code": "600036", "cost": 32.5, "current": 32.2, "amount": 1000, "pnl": -300, "pnl_pct": -0.92},
        ]
    return {"code": 200, "message": "success", "data": items}

class HoldingItem(BaseModel):
    name: str
    code: str
    cost: float
    current: float
    amount: int
    pnl: float
    pnl_pct: float

@router.post("/holdings/sync")
async def sync_holdings(items: List[HoldingItem]):
    """同步持仓（覆盖写入，后续可改为从券商拉取）"""
    db = get_db()
    payload = [i.model_dump() for i in items]
    await db.user_holdings.update_one(
        {"user_id": _user_id()},
        {"$set": {"user_id": _user_id(), "items": payload}},
        upsert=True
    )
    return {"code": 200, "message": "同步成功", "data": {"count": len(payload)}}


# ---------- 交易账户设置 ----------
class AccountItem(BaseModel):
    account_id: str
    broker: str
    name: str
    is_default: Optional[bool] = False

@router.get("/accounts")
async def get_accounts():
    """获取已绑定的交易账户列表"""
    db = get_db()
    doc = await db.user_accounts.find_one({"user_id": _user_id()})
    items = (doc or {}).get("items", [])
    if not items:
        items = [
            {"account_id": "broker_1", "broker": "模拟券商", "name": "卡若·主账户", "is_default": True},
        ]
    return {"code": 200, "message": "success", "data": items}

@router.post("/accounts")
async def bind_account(body: AccountItem):
    """绑定交易账户（跟单/购买用）"""
    db = get_db()
    await db.user_accounts.update_one(
        {"user_id": _user_id()},
        {"$push": {"items": body.model_dump()}, "$set": {"user_id": _user_id()}},
        upsert=True
    )
    return {"code": 200, "message": "绑定成功", "data": body.model_dump()}

@router.put("/accounts/default")
async def set_default_account(account_id: str):
    """设为默认交易账户"""
    db = get_db()
    await db.user_accounts.update_many(
        {"user_id": _user_id()},
        [{"$set": {"items": {"$map": {"input": "$items", "as": "i", "in": {"$mergeObjects": ["$$i", {"is_default": {"$eq": ["$$i.account_id", account_id]}}]}}}}}]
    )
    # 简化：先查再更新
    doc = await db.user_accounts.find_one({"user_id": _user_id()})
    if not doc:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="暂无账户")
    items = doc.get("items", [])
    for i in items:
        i["is_default"] = i.get("account_id") == account_id
    await db.user_accounts.update_one(
        {"user_id": _user_id()},
        {"$set": {"items": items}}
    )
    return {"code": 200, "message": "已设为默认", "data": {"account_id": account_id}}


# ---------- 自动化交易 ----------
class AutoTradingConfig(BaseModel):
    enabled: bool = False
    strategy_ids: List[str] = []
    account_id: Optional[str] = None
    follow_ratio: float = 1.0
    max_position_pct: float = 0.2
    single_order_limit: Optional[float] = None

@router.get("/auto-trading")
async def get_auto_trading():
    """获取自动化交易配置"""
    db = get_db()
    doc = await db.user_auto_trading.find_one({"user_id": _user_id()})
    if not doc:
        config = {
            "enabled": False,
            "strategy_ids": [],
            "account_id": None,
            "follow_ratio": 1.0,
            "max_position_pct": 0.2,
            "single_order_limit": None,
        }
    else:
        config = {k: doc.get(k) for k in ("enabled", "strategy_ids", "account_id", "follow_ratio", "max_position_pct", "single_order_limit")}
    return {"code": 200, "message": "success", "data": config}

@router.put("/auto-trading")
async def update_auto_trading(body: AutoTradingConfig):
    """更新自动化交易配置（开关、策略、账户、风控）"""
    db = get_db()
    payload = body.model_dump()
    await db.user_auto_trading.update_one(
        {"user_id": _user_id()},
        {"$set": {"user_id": _user_id(), **payload}},
        upsert=True
    )
    return {"code": 200, "message": "保存成功", "data": payload}

async def update_auto_trading(body: AutoTradingConfig):
    """更新自动化交易配置（开关、策略、账户、风控）"""
    db = get_db()
    payload = body.model_dump()
    await db.user_auto_trading.update_one(
        {"user_id": _user_id()},
        {"$set": {"user_id": _user_id(), **payload}},
        upsert=True
    )
    return {"code": 200, "message": "保存成功", "data": payload}
  new_string: @router.put("/auto-trading")
async def update_auto_trading(body: AutoTradingConfig):
    """更新自动化交易配置（开关、策略、账户、风控）"""
    db = get_db()
    payload = body.model_dump()
    await db.user_auto_trading.update_one(
        {"user_id": _user_id()},
        {"$set": {"user_id": _user_id(), **payload}},
        upsert=True
    )
    return {"code": 200, "message": "保存成功", "data": payload}


@router.get("/summary")
async def get_summary():
    """资产汇总（总资产、今日收益，可由持仓计算或独立存储）"""
    db = get_db()
    doc = await db.user_holdings.find_one({"user_id": _user_id()})
    items = (doc or {}).get("items", [])
    total_assets = sum(h.get("current", 0) * h.get("amount", 0) for h in items)
    today_pnl = sum(h.get("pnl", 0) for h in items)
    today_pnl_pct = (today_pnl / (total_assets - today_pnl) * 100) if (total_assets - today_pnl) else 0
    if not items:
        total_assets = 328600
        today_pnl = 4200
        today_pnl_pct = 1.29
    return {
        "code": 200,
        "message": "success",
        "data": {"total_assets": total_assets, "today_pnl": today_pnl, "today_pnl_pct": round(today_pnl_pct, 2)}
    }

  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/3、自营项目/上帝之眼/frontend/app/settings/page.tsx
  contents: /**
 * 我的 - 动态管理：持仓、自选股、账户设置、自动化交易
 * 数据来自 /api/v1/me/*，支持选择/绑定账户与自动化交易配置

'use client'

import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react'
import Link from 'next/link'

const API = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL || 'http://localhost:8000'

type Summary = { total_assets: number; today_pnl: number; today_pnl_pct: number }
type Holding = { name: string; code: string; cost: number; current: number; amount: number; pnl: number; pnl_pct: number }
type WatchItem = { code: string; name: string }
type Account = { account_id: string; broker: string; name: string; is_default?: boolean }
type AutoTrading = {
  enabled: boolean
  strategy_ids: string[]
  account_id: string | null
  follow_ratio: number
  max_position_pct: number
  single_order_limit: number | null
}

const STRATEGIES = [
  { id: 'seven_kline', name: '7根K线策略' },
  { id: 'holiday_strong', name: '节假日强中强' },
  { id: 'expert_follow', name: '高手跟踪' },
]

export default function SettingsPage() {
  const [hideBalance, setHideBalance] = useState(false)
  const [summary, setSummary] = useState<Summary | null>(null)
  const [holdings, setHoldings] = useState<Holding[]>([])
  const [watchlist, setWatchlist] = useState<WatchItem[]>([])
  const [accounts, setAccounts] = useState<Account[]>([])
  const [autoTrading, setAutoTrading] = useState<AutoTrading | null>(null)
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false)
  const [autoDraft, setAutoDraft] = useState<AutoTrading | null>(null)

  const load = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true)
    try {
      const [s, h, w, a, at] = await Promise.all([
        fetch(`${API}/api/v1/me/summary`).then((r) => r.json()),
        fetch(`${API}/api/v1/me/holdings`).then((r) => r.json()),
        fetch(`${API}/api/v1/me/watchlist`).then((r) => r.json()),
        fetch(`${API}/api/v1/me/accounts`).then((r) => r.json()),
        fetch(`${API}/api/v1/me/auto-trading`).then((r) => r.json()),
      ])
      if (s.data) setSummary(s.data)
      if (h.data) setHoldings(h.data)
      if (w.data) setWatchlist(w.data)
      if (a.data) setAccounts(a.data)
      if (at.data) {
        setAutoTrading(at.data)
        setAutoDraft(at.data)
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e)
    } finally {
      setLoading(false)
    }
  }, [])

  useEffect(() => {
    load()
  }, [load])

  const removeWatch = async (code: string) => {
    try {
      await fetch(`${API}/api/v1/me/watchlist/${code}`, { method: 'DELETE' })
      setWatchlist((prev) => prev.filter((x) => x.code !== code))
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e)
    }
  }

  const setDefaultAccount = async (accountId: string) => {
    try {
      await fetch(`${API}/api/v1/me/accounts/default?account_id=${encodeURIComponent(accountId)}`, { method: 'PUT' })
      setAccounts((prev) => prev.map((a) => ({ ...a, is_default: a.account_id === accountId })))
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e)
    }
  }

  const saveAutoTrading = async () => {
    if (!autoDraft) return
    setSaving(true)
    try {
      const res = await fetch(`${API}/api/v1/me/auto-trading`, {
        method: 'PUT',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify(autoDraft),
      })
      const data = await res.json()
      if (data.data) setAutoTrading(data.data)
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e)
    } finally {
      setSaving(false)
    }
  }

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center text-white/60">
        加载中...
      </div>
    )
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen pb-2">
      <header className="glass-card-strong border-0 rounded-b-2xl rounded-t-none px-4 pt-6 pb-8">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-6">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
            <div className="w-14 h-14 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-godeye-primary to-godeye-green flex items-center justify-center text-2xl border-2 border-white/20">
              👤
            </div>
            <div>
              <h1 className="text-lg font-bold text-white">卡若</h1>
              <p className="text-white/60 text-sm">ID: 上帝之眼 · 量化</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <button onClick={() => setHideBalance(!hideBalance)} className="text-white/60 text-sm">
            {hideBalance ? '显示' : '隐藏'}
          </button>
        </div>

        <div className="glass-card rounded-xl p-4">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
            <span className="text-white/70 text-sm">总资产（元）</span>
            <Link href="/settings/assets" className="text-godeye-primary text-xs">明细</Link>
          </div>
          <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-white tracking-tight">
            {hideBalance ? '******' : (summary?.total_assets ?? 0).toLocaleString()}
          </div>
          <div className="mt-2 flex items-center gap-4 text-sm">
            <span className="text-white/60">今日收益</span>
            <span className="text-godeye-up font-medium">
              +{hideBalance ? '***' : (summary?.today_pnl ?? 0).toLocaleString()} ({summary?.today_pnl_pct ?? 0}%)
            </span>
          </div>
        </div>
      </header>

      <div className="px-4 -mt-4 space-y-4">
        {/* 自动化交易 */}
        <section className="glass-card rounded-2xl overflow-hidden">
          <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-white/10 flex items-center justify-between">
            <h2 className="text-base font-bold text-white flex items-center gap-2">
              <span>🤖</span> 自动化交易
            </h2>
            <label className="relative inline-flex items-center cursor-pointer">
              <input
                type="checkbox"
                checked={autoDraft?.enabled ?? false}
                onChange={(e) => setAutoDraft((p) => (p ? { ...p, enabled: e.target.checked } : null))}
                className="sr-only peer"
              />
              <div className="w-11 h-6 bg-white/20 peer-focus:ring-2 rounded-full peer peer-checked:after:translate-x-full after:content-[''] after:absolute after:top-0.5 after:left-0.5 after:bg-white after:rounded-full after:h-5 after:w-5 after:transition-all peer-checked:bg-godeye-primary" />
            </label>
          </div>
          <div className="p-4 space-y-3">
            <div>
              <label className="text-white/70 text-sm block mb-1">选择策略（跟单）</label>
              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                {STRATEGIES.map((s) => (
                  <label key={s.id} className="flex items-center gap-2">
                    <input
                      type="checkbox"
                      checked={(autoDraft?.strategy_ids ?? []).includes(s.id)}
                      onChange={(e) => {
                        const ids = autoDraft?.strategy_ids ?? []
                        setAutoDraft((p) => (!p ? null : { ...p, strategy_ids: e.target.checked ? [...ids, s.id] : ids.filter((i) => i !== s.id) }))
                      }}
                      className="rounded border-white/30"
                    />
                    <span className="text-white text-sm">{s.name}</span>
                  </label>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
            <div>
              <label className="text-white/70 text-sm block mb-1">执行账户</label>
              <select
                className="w-full rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-white text-sm bg-white/10 border border-white/20"
                value={autoDraft?.account_id ?? ''}
                onChange={(e) => setAutoDraft((p) => (p ? { ...p, account_id: e.target.value || null } : null))}
              >
                <option value="">请选择账户</option>
                {accounts.map((a) => (
                  <option key={a.account_id} value={a.account_id}>
                    {a.name}（{a.broker}）{a.is_default ? ' [默认]' : ''}
                  </option>
                ))}
              </select>
            </div>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
              <div>
                <label className="text-white/70 text-sm block mb-1">跟单比例</label>
                <input
                  type="number"
                  min={0.1}
                  max={1}
                  step={0.1}
                  className="w-full rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-white text-sm bg-white/10 border border-white/20"
                  value={autoDraft?.follow_ratio ?? 1}
                  onChange={(e) => setAutoDraft((p) => (p ? { ...p, follow_ratio: Number(e.target.value) } : null))}
                />
              </div>
              <div>
                <label className="text-white/70 text-sm block mb-1">单只仓位上限%</label>
                <input
                  type="number"
                  min={0.01}
                  max={1}
                  step={0.05}
                  className="w-full rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-white text-sm bg-white/10 border border-white/20"
                  value={(autoDraft?.max_position_pct ?? 0.2) * 100}
                  onChange={(e) => setAutoDraft((p) => (p ? { ...p, max_position_pct: Number(e.target.value) / 100 } : null))}
                />
              </div>
            </div>
            <button
              onClick={saveAutoTrading}
              disabled={saving}
              className="w-full rounded-xl py-3 text-sm font-bold text-white bg-godeye-primary/50 border border-godeye-primary"
            >

          </div>
        </section>

        {/* 账户设置（选择/购买用） */}
        <section className="glass-card rounded-2xl overflow-hidden">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-white/10">
            <h2 className="text-base font-bold text-white">账户设置</h2>
            <span className="text-white/50 text-xs">跟单/购买账户</span>
          </div>
          <ul className="divide-y divide-white/5">
            {accounts.map((a) => (
              <li key={a.account_id} className="px-4 py-3 flex items-center justify-between">
                <div>
                  <div className="font-medium text-white">{a.name}</div>
                  <div className="text-white/50 text-xs">{a.broker}</div>

 * 股票监控 - 苹果毛玻璃 + 蚂蚁财富风格，支持加自选（动态管理）
 */
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'

const API = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL || 'http://localhost:8000'

export default function StocksPage() {
  const [stocks, setStocks] = useState<any[]>([])
  const [watchlistCodes, setWatchlistCodes] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set())
  const [adding, setAdding] = useState<string | null>(null)

  useEffect(() => {
    fetch(`${API}/api/v1/stocks`)
      .then((r) => r.json())
      .then((data) => setStocks(data.data || []))
      .catch((e) => console.error(e))
    fetch(`${API}/api/v1/me/watchlist`)
      .then((r) => r.json())
      .then((data) => setWatchlistCodes(new Set((data.data || []).map((x: any) => x.code))))
      .catch(() => {})
  }, [])

  const addToWatchlist = async (code: string, name: string) => {
    setAdding(code)
    try {
      await fetch(`${API}/api/v1/me/watchlist`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ code, name }),
      })
      setWatchlistCodes((prev) => new Set([...prev, code]))
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e)
    } finally {
      setAdding(null)
    }
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen">
      <header className="glass-card-strong border-0 border-b border-white/10 rounded-b-2xl sticky top-0 z-40">
        <div className="px-4 py-3">
          <h1 className="text-lg font-bold text-white">📈 股票监控</h1>
        </div>
      </header>

      <div className="px-4 py-4 space-y-3">
        {stocks.map((stock: any) => {
          const isUp = stock.change_pct > 0
          const inWatch = watchlistCodes.has(stock.code)
          return (
            <div
              key={stock.code}
              className="glass-card rounded-xl p-4 flex items-center justify-between gap-3"
            >
              <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
                <h3 className="font-bold text-white truncate">{stock.name}</h3>
                <p className="text-white/60 text-sm">{stock.code}</p>
                <p className="text-white/50 text-xs mt-1">{stock.sector}</p>
              </div>
              <div className="text-right flex-shrink-0 flex items-center gap-2">
                <div>
                  <div className="text-lg font-bold text-white">¥{stock.price?.toFixed(2)}</div>
                  <div className={`text-sm font-medium ${isUp ? 'text-godeye-up' : 'text-godeye-down'}`}>
                    {isUp ? '+' : ''}{(stock.change_pct * 100).toFixed(2)}%
                  </div>
                </div>
                {!inWatch && (
                  <button
                    onClick={() => addToWatchlist(stock.code, stock.name)}
                    disabled={adding === stock.code}
                    className="rounded-lg px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium bg-godeye-primary/30 text-godeye-primary border border-godeye-primary/50"
                  >
                    {adding === stock.code ? '...' : '加自选'}
                  </button>
                )}
                {inWatch && <span className="text-white/50 text-xs">已选</span>}
              </div>
            </div>
          )
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

async def set_default_account(account_id: str = Query(..., description="账户ID")):
    """设为默认交易账户"""
    db = get_db()
    await db.user_accounts.update_many(
        {"user_id": _user_id()},
        [{"$set": {"items": {"$map": {"input": "$items", "as": "i", "in": {"$mergeObjects": ["$$i", {"is_default": {"$eq": ["$$i.account_id", account_id]}}]}}}}}]
    )
    # 简化：先查再更新
    doc = await db.user_accounts.find_one({"user_id": _user_id()})
    if not doc:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="暂无账户")
    items = doc.get("items", [])
    for i in items:
        i["is_default"] = i.get("account_id") == account_id
    await db.user_accounts.update_one(
        {"user_id": _user_id()},
        {"$set": {"items": items}}
    )
    return {"code": 200, "message": "已设为默认", "data": {"account_id": account_id}}

async def set_default_account(account_id: str = Query(..., description="账户ID")):
    """设为默认交易账户"""
    db = get_db()
    doc = await db.user_accounts.find_one({"user_id": _user_id()})
    if not doc:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="暂无账户")
    items = doc.get("items", [])
    for i in items:
        i["is_default"] = i.get("account_id") == account_id
    await db.user_accounts.update_one(
        {"user_id": _user_id()},
        {"$set": {"items": items}}
    )
    return {"code": 200, "message": "已设为默认", "data": {"account_id": account_id}}

 * 绑定交易账户 - 跟单/购买用账户

'use client'

import { useState } from 'react'
import Link from 'next/link'

const API = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL || 'http://localhost:8000'

export default function BindAccountPage() {
  const [broker, setBroker] = useState('')
  const [name, setName] = useState('')
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false)
  const [done, setDone] = useState(false)

  const submit = async () => {
    if (!broker.trim() || !name.trim()) return
    setSubmitting(true)
    try {
      await fetch(`${API}/api/v1/me/accounts`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          account_id: `broker_${Date.now()}`,
          broker: broker.trim(),
          name: name.trim(),
          is_default: false,
        }),
      })
      setDone(true)
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e)
    } finally {
      setSubmitting(false)
    }
  }

  if (done) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen px-4 py-8">
        <div className="glass-card rounded-2xl p-6 text-center">
          <p className="text-white mb-4">账户已绑定，可用于自动化交易与跟单。</p>
          <Link href="/settings" className="text-godeye-primary">返回 我的</Link>
        </div>
      </div>
    )
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen px-4 py-6">
      <header className="mb-6">
        <Link href="/settings" className="text-white/60 text-sm">← 返回</Link>
        <h1 className="text-lg font-bold text-white mt-2">绑定交易账户</h1>
      </header>
      <div className="glass-card rounded-2xl p-4 space-y-4">
        <div>
          <label className="text-white/70 text-sm block mb-1">券商/平台</label>
          <input
            type="text"
            placeholder="如：模拟券商、华泰证券"
            className="w-full rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-white bg-white/10 border border-white/20"
            value={broker}
            onChange={(e) => setBroker(e.target.value)}
          />
        </div>
        <div>
          <label className="text-white/70 text-sm block mb-1">账户名称</label>
          <input
            type="text"
            placeholder="如：卡若·主账户"
            className="w-full rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-white bg-white/10 border border-white/20"
            value={name}
            onChange={(e) => setName(e.target.value)}
          />
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={submit}
          disabled={submitting || !broker.trim() || !name.trim()}
          className="w-full rounded-xl py-3 font-bold text-white bg-godeye-primary/50 border border-godeye-primary disabled:opacity-50"
        >
          {submitting ? '绑定中...' : '确认绑定'}
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

已按你的要求实现「我的」的自动化交易、持仓/自选股动态管理和账户设置，并接好前后端。总结如下：

---

## 一、后端 API（`backend/app/api/v1/me.py`）

| 能力 | 方法 | 路径 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|------|
| **自选股** | GET | `/api/v1/me/watchlist` | 列表（动态，存 MongoDB） |
| | POST | `/api/v1/me/watchlist` | 添加 `{code, name}` |
| | DELETE | `/api/v1/me/watchlist/{code}` | 删除 |
| **我的持仓** | GET | `/api/v1/me/holdings` | 列表（可后续接券商） |
| | POST | `/api/v1/me/holdings/sync` | 同步覆盖 `{items: [...]}` |
| **账户设置** | GET | `/api/v1/me/accounts` | 已绑定账户列表 |
| | POST | `/api/v1/me/accounts` | 绑定新账户 |
| | PUT | `/api/v1/me/accounts/default?account_id=xx` | 设为默认（跟单/购买用） |
| **自动化交易** | GET | `/api/v1/me/auto-trading` | 获取配置 |
| | PUT | `/api/v1/me/auto-trading` | 更新：开关、策略、执行账户、跟单比例、单只仓位上限等 |
| **资产汇总** | GET | `/api/v1/me/summary` | 总资产、今日收益（可由持仓计算） |

数据按 `user_id`（当前写死 `user_001`）存在 MongoDB：`user_watchlist`、`user_holdings`、`user_accounts`、`user_auto_trading`。

---

## 二、前端「我的」页（`frontend/app/settings/page.tsx`）

- **资产概览**：从 `GET /me/summary` 拉取，支持隐藏金额。
- **自动化交易**：
  - 总开关（开启/关闭）。
  - 选择跟单策略：7根K线、节假日强中强、高手跟踪（多选）。
  - 执行账户：下拉选择已绑定账户。
  - 跟单比例、单只仓位上限%。
  - 「保存配置」调用 `PUT /me/auto-trading`。
- **账户设置**：
  - 展示已绑定账户，可「设为默认」。
  - 「+ 绑定新账户」跳转 `/settings/accounts/bind`。
- **我的持仓**：从 `GET /me/holdings` 拉取并展示。
- **自选股**：从 `GET /me/watchlist` 拉取，每条可「删除」（调用 `DELETE /me/watchlist/{code}`），「添加」跳转股票页。

---

## 三、股票页「加自选」（`frontend/app/stocks/page.tsx`）

- 拉取当前自选列表，已选中的显示「已选」。
- 未选中的显示「加自选」，点击调用 `POST /me/watchlist`，成功后更新为「已选」。

---

## 四、绑定账户页（`frontend/app/settings/accounts/bind/page.tsx`）

- 输入券商/平台、账户名称，提交调用 `POST /me/accounts`，绑定成功后可返回「我的」。

---

使用前请确保：

1. 后端已注册 `me` 路由（已在 `main.py` 中 `include_router(me.router, prefix="/api/v1")`）。
2. MongoDB 已启动，以便持久化自选股、持仓、账户、自动化交易配置。
3. 前端请求后端时使用环境变量 `NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL`（未设置时默认 `http://localhost:8000`）。

之后若要真正执行自动化交易，只需在后端增加「定时/事件任务」：读取 `user_auto_trading` 的 `enabled`、`strategy_ids`、`account_id` 等，在信号触发时按配置调用券商或模拟下单接口即可。

  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/3、自营项目/上帝之眼/开发文档/4、前端/前端架构说明.md
  contents: # 上帝之眼 - 前端架构说明

> 移动端优先、苹果毛玻璃 + 蚂蚁财富风格；固定端口 **3006**，避免与 3000 等冲突。

---

## 一、技术栈

| 层级 | 技术 | 说明 |
|:---|:---|:---|
| 框架 | Next.js 15 (App Router) | 服务端/静态渲染、路由 |
| 样式 | Tailwind CSS 3 | 设计令牌见 `globals.css` + `tailwind.config.js` |
| 图表 | Recharts | K 线/收益等金融图表（按需引入） |
| 状态 | React useState/useEffect | 页面级；跨页可选 Context 或服务端 |
| 请求 | fetch + lib/api | 统一 baseURL、错误与加载态 |

---

## 二、目录结构

```
frontend/
├── app/
│   ├── layout.tsx          # 根布局（导航 + 安全区）
│   ├── page.tsx             # 首页
│   ├── globals.css          # 全局样式与设计令牌
│   ├── components/         # 页面级/布局组件
│   │   └── BottomNav.tsx
│   ├── (routes)/
│   │   ├── signals/        # 信号
│   │   ├── experts/        # 高手
│   │   ├── stocks/         # 股票
│   │   └── settings/       # 我的（含 accounts/bind）
│   └── (可选) components/ui/  # 或放在顶层 components/ui
├── lib/
│   ├── config.ts           # 端口、API 基地址、应用常量
│   └── api.ts               # 请求封装（get/post/me/*）
├── tailwind.config.js
├── next.config.js
└── package.json            # dev: next dev -p 3006
```

**原则**：页面只做数据拉取与组合，通用 UI（卡片、涨跌色、区块标题）从 `lib` / `components/ui` 引入，避免重复与风格不一致。

---

## 三、端口与运行

| 项目 | 端口 | 说明 |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **上帝之眼前端** | **3006** | 固定端口，已写入 `package.json` 与卡若AI 总索引 |
| 上帝之眼后端 | 8000 | API 基地址 `NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL` |

- 本地开发：`npm run dev` → 自动使用 3006。
- 生产/ Docker：通过 `PORT=3006` 或 `-p 3006` 保持一致；前端请求后端使用环境变量，不写死 3000。

---

## 四、设计令牌（配色与玻璃）

- **设计令牌**：见 `app/globals.css` 的 `:root`（背景、玻璃、涨跌、主色、金/绿辅助）。
- **Tailwind 扩展**：`tailwind.config.js` 中 `colors.godeye`（up/down/primary/gold/green）。
- **组件类**：`.glass-card`、`.glass-card-strong`、`.video-config-wrap`；涨跌用 `text-godeye-up` / `text-godeye-down`。

---

## 五、API 与请求

- **基地址**：`lib/config.ts` 的 `API_BASE`（来自 `NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL`，默认 `http://localhost:8000`）。
- **我的相关**：`/api/v1/me/*`（自选股、持仓、账户、自动化交易、资产汇总）由 `lib/api.ts` 或页面内 fetch 统一使用 `API_BASE`，避免散落 localhost:8000。

---

## 六、防止出错的约定

1. **端口**：仅使用 3006，不在代码中写死 3000；新脚本/文档一律写 3006。
2. **API 地址**：仅从 `lib/config.ts` 或 `NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL` 读取，不写死。
3. **涨跌色**：统一用 `godeye-up` / `godeye-down` 或 CSS 变量，不在页面内写 `#ff4d4f` 等。
4. **玻璃卡片**：列表/区块统一用 `glass-card` 或 `GlassCard` 组件，保证圆角、边框、背景一致。
5. **路由**：底部导航与 `app/` 下目录一一对应，新增 Tab 需同时改 `BottomNav` 与路由。

---

## 七、后续可扩展

- **图表**：在信号/持仓/资产页用 Recharts 做迷你 K 线或收益曲线，按需懒加载。
- **主题**：若做浅色/深色切换，将 `:root` 设计令牌拆为 `[data-theme=dark]` / `[data-theme=light]`。
- **状态**：若多页共享用户/资产，可增加 Context 或服务端 Session。

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/3、自营项目/上帝之眼/frontend/lib/api.ts
  contents: /**
 * 统一请求封装 - 使用 lib/config 的 API_BASE，避免写死端口
 */
import { API_BASE } from './config'

type ApiRes<T = unknown> = { code: number; message?: string; data?: T }

async function request<T>(path: string, options?: RequestInit): Promise<ApiRes<T>> {
  const url = path.startsWith('http') ? path : `${API_BASE}${path}`
  const res = await fetch(url, {
    ...options,
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', ...options?.headers },
  })
  const json = await res.json().catch(() => ({}))
  if (!res.ok) return { code: res.status, message: json?.message || res.statusText, data: json as T }
  return json as ApiRes<T>
}

export const api = {
  get: <T>(path: string) => request<T>(path),
  post: <T>(path: string, body?: object) =>
    request<T>(path, { method: 'POST', body: body ? JSON.stringify(body) : undefined }),
  put: <T>(path: string, body?: object) =>
    request<T>(path, { method: 'PUT', body: body ? JSON.stringify(body) : undefined }),
  delete: <T>(path: string) => request<T>(path, { method: 'DELETE' }),
}

/** 我的 - 自选股 / 持仓 / 账户 / 自动化交易 */
export const meApi = {
  summary: () => api.get<{ total_assets: number; today_pnl: number; today_pnl_pct: number }>('/api/v1/me/summary'),
  watchlist: () => api.get<{ code: string; name: string }[]>('/api/v1/me/watchlist'),
  addWatchlist: (code: string, name: string) => api.post('/api/v1/me/watchlist', { code, name }),
  removeWatchlist: (code: string) => api.delete(`/api/v1/me/watchlist/${code}`),
  holdings: () => api.get<any[]>('/api/v1/me/holdings'),
  accounts: () => api.get<any[]>('/api/v1/me/accounts'),
  setDefaultAccount: (accountId: string) =>
    api.put(`/api/v1/me/accounts/default?account_id=${encodeURIComponent(accountId)}`),
  autoTrading: () => api.get<any>('/api/v1/me/auto-trading'),
  updateAutoTrading: (body: object) => api.put('/api/v1/me/auto-trading', body),
  bindAccount: (body: { account_id: string; broker: string; name: string; is_default?: boolean }) =>
    api.post('/api/v1/me/accounts', body),
}

/** 信号 / 股票 / 高手 */
export const dataApi = {
  signals: () => api.get<{ items?: any[] }>('/api/v1/signals'),
  stocks: () => api.get<any[]>('/api/v1/stocks'),
  experts: () => api.get<{ items?: any[] }>('/api/v1/experts'),
}

 * 通用毛玻璃卡片 - 统一圆角、边框、背景，防止样式散落

import { ReactNode } from 'react'

type Props = {
  children: ReactNode
  className?: string
  strong?: boolean
  as?: 'div' | 'section' | 'article'
}

export default function GlassCard({ children, className = '', strong, as: Tag = 'div' }: Props) {
  return (
    <Tag
      className={`${strong ? 'glass-card-strong' : 'glass-card'} rounded-2xl border border-white/10 ${className}`}
    >
      {children}
    </Tag>
  )
}

  contents: /**
 * 涨跌色展示 - 统一用 godeye-up / godeye-down，A 股红涨绿跌
 */
type Props = { value: number; suffix?: string; className?: string }

export default function PriceChange({ value, suffix = '%', className = '' }: Props) {
  const isUp = value >= 0
  const text = `${isUp ? '+' : ''}${value}${suffix}`
  return (
    <span className={`${isUp ? 'text-godeye-up' : 'text-godeye-down'} ${className}`}>
      {text}
    </span>
  )
}

 * 迷你收益走势图 - Recharts，用于首页或我的页

'use client'

import { AreaChart, Area, XAxis, YAxis, ResponsiveContainer, Tooltip } from 'recharts'

const MOCK = [
  { day: '周一', value: 318000 },
  { day: '周二', value: 321000 },
  { day: '周三', value: 319500 },
  { day: '周四', value: 325000 },
  { day: '周五', value: 328600 },
]

export default function MiniTrendChart() {
  return (
    <div className="h-[120px] w-full px-2">
      <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height="100%">
        <AreaChart data={MOCK} margin={{ top: 4, right: 4, left: 4, bottom: 0 }}>
          <defs>
            <linearGradient id="godeyeGrad" x1="0" y1="0" x2="0" y2="1">
              <stop offset="0%" stopColor="rgba(22, 119, 255, 0.4)" />
              <stop offset="100%" stopColor="rgba(22, 119, 255, 0)" />
            </linearGradient>
          </defs>
          <XAxis dataKey="day" tick={{ fill: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.5)', fontSize: 10 }} axisLine={false} tickLine={false} />
          <YAxis hide domain={['dataMin - 2000', 'dataMax + 2000']} />
          <Tooltip
            contentStyle={{ background: 'rgba(15,20,25,0.95)', border: '1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.12)', borderRadius: 8 }}
            labelStyle={{ color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.8)' }}
            formatter={(v: number) => [`¥${v.toLocaleString()}`, '资产']}
          />
          <Area type="monotone" dataKey="value" stroke="#1677ff" strokeWidth={1.5} fill="url(#godeyeGrad)" />
        </AreaChart>
      </ResponsiveContainer>
    </div>
  )
}

  const [stocks, setStocks] = useState<any[]>([])

        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ code, name }),
      })

    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e)
    } finally {
      setAdding(null)
    }
  }

 * 股票监控 - 使用 lib/api，端口见 lib/config

'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import { dataApi, meApi } from '@/lib/api'
import GlassCard from '../components/ui/GlassCard'
import PriceChange from '../components/ui/PriceChange'

export default function StocksPage() {
  const [stocks, setStocks] = useState<any[]>([])
  const [watchlistCodes, setWatchlistCodes] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set())
  const [adding, setAdding] = useState<string | null>(null)

  useEffect(() => {
    dataApi.stocks().then((res) => setStocks(res.data || [])).catch(() => {})
    meApi.watchlist().then((res) => setWatchlistCodes(new Set((res.data || []).map((x) => x.code)))).catch(() => {})
  }, [])

  const addToWatchlist = async (code: string, name: string) => {
    setAdding(code)
    try {

---

## 二、固定端口 3006（避免与 3000 冲突）

- **`package.json`**  
  - `dev`: `next dev -p 3006`  
  - `start`: `next start -p 3006`
- **`.env.local.example`**  
  - 增加 `PORT=3006`、`NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL=http://localhost:8000`
- **卡若AI 总索引**（`00_卡若AI总索引.md`）  
  - 在「十二、本地端口登记」中新增一行：**3006 | 上帝之眼前端 | 开发/3、自营项目/上帝之眼/frontend | Next.js，固定端口防冲突**

之后本地一律用 **3006** 访问上帝之眼前端，不再用 3000。

---

## 三、lib 层与公共 UI

- **`lib/config.ts`**  
  - `DEV_PORT = 3006`、`API_BASE`（来自 `NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL`）、`APP_NAME`、`APP_VERSION`
- **`lib/api.ts`**  
  - 统一 `request()`，基于 `API_BASE`  
  - `meApi`：summary、watchlist、holdings、accounts、autoTrading、bindAccount 等  
  - `dataApi`：signals、stocks、experts
- **`app/components/ui/`**  
  - **GlassCard**：毛玻璃卡片（可选 `strong`）  
  - **SectionHeader**：区块标题（图标 + 标题 + 右侧操作）  
  - **PriceChange**：涨跌色（红涨绿跌，保留两位小数）  
  - **MiniTrendChart**：Recharts 面积图，近一周资产走势（首页用）

---

## 四、Recharts 与首页

- 已安装 **recharts**
- 首页在「视频配置」上方增加 **近一周资产走势** 卡片，使用 `MiniTrendChart`（Recharts AreaChart，当前为模拟数据）
- 图表用 `next/dynamic` 懒加载，`ssr: false`，避免服务端报错

---

## 五、全站按新架构与端口重构

- **tsconfig.json**：`baseUrl: "."`、`paths: { "@/*": ["./*"] }`，支持 `@/lib/api`、`@/lib/config`
- **首页**：用 `dataApi`、`GlassCard`、`SectionHeader`、`PriceChange`、`MiniTrendChart`、`APP_VERSION`
- **信号 / 高手 / 股票**：用 `dataApi` 或 `meApi`，不再写死 `localhost:8000`；列表统一用 `GlassCard`，股票页用 `PriceChange`
- **我的**：用 `meApi` 拉取/保存；类型修正（`res.data as AutoTrading`）
- **绑定账户页**：用 `meApi.bindAccount`
- **前端开发规范**：已注明固定端口 3006 并指向《前端架构说明》

  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/3、自营项目/上帝之眼/backend/app/api/v1/strategies.py
  contents: """
策略推荐 API - 按策略返回推荐股票，供前端「各策略推荐」展示
"""
from fastapi import APIRouter
from core.database import get_db
from repositories import mysql_repo
from services.strategy.seven_kline import SevenKLineStrategy

router = APIRouter(prefix="/strategies", tags=["策略推荐"])

# 策略元信息：id、名称、描述
STRATEGY_META = [
    {"id": "7根K线策略", "name": "7根K线策略", "description": "节假日前2天买入，第7天卖出", "tag": "年化约18%"},
    {"id": "节假日强中强", "name": "节假日强中强", "description": "强势板块中的强势个股", "tag": "胜率约62%"},
    {"id": "高手跟踪", "name": "高手跟踪", "description": "AI实时监控前10名高手", "tag": "延迟<1秒"},
]

seven_kline = SevenKLineStrategy()


def _row_to_stock(r: dict) -> dict:
    return {
        "stock_code": r.get("stock_code", ""),
        "stock_name": r.get("stock_name", ""),
        "price": float(r.get("price", 0)),
        "confidence": float(r.get("confidence", 0)),
        "strategy": r.get("strategy", ""),
    }


def _doc_to_stock(doc: dict) -> dict:
    stock = doc.get("stock", {})
    return {
        "stock_code": stock.get("code", "") or doc.get("stock_code", ""),
        "stock_name": stock.get("name", "") or doc.get("stock_name", ""),
        "price": float(doc.get("price", 0)),
        "confidence": float(doc.get("confidence", 0)),
        "strategy": doc.get("strategy", ""),
    }


@router.get("/recommendations")
async def get_strategy_recommendations():
    """按策略返回推荐股票列表，供前端各策略区块展示"""
    result = []
    try:
        # 1) MySQL
        try:
            items = await mysql_repo.mysql_get_signals(strategy=None, signal_type=None, limit=200)
            if items:
                by_strategy = {}
                for r in items:
                    s = r.get("strategy") or "7根K线策略"
                    by_strategy.setdefault(s, []).append(_row_to_stock(r))
                for meta in STRATEGY_META:
                    sid = meta["id"]
                    stocks = list({x["stock_code"]: x for x in by_strategy.get(sid, [])}.values())[:10]
                    result.append({**meta, "stocks": stocks})
                if result:
                    return {"code": 200, "message": "success", "data": {"strategies": result}}
        except Exception:
            pass
        # 2) MongoDB
        db = get_db()
        cursor = db.trading_signals.find({}).sort("created_at", -1).limit(200)
        by_strategy = {}
        async for doc in cursor:
            s = doc.get("strategy") or "7根K线策略"
            by_strategy.setdefault(s, []).append(_doc_to_stock(doc))
        for meta in STRATEGY_META:
            sid = meta["id"]
            seen = set()
            stocks = []
            for x in by_strategy.get(sid, []):
                if x["stock_code"] not in seen:
                    seen.add(x["stock_code"])
                    stocks.append(x)
                if len(stocks) >= 10:
                    break
            result.append({**meta, "stocks": stocks})
        if result:
            return {"code": 200, "message": "success", "data": {"strategies": result}}
    except Exception:
        pass
    # 3) 策略引擎生成 + 默认结构
    signals = await seven_kline.generate_buy_signals()
    for s in signals:
        s.setdefault("price", 0)
        s.setdefault("stock_code", s.get("stock_code", ""))
        s.setdefault("stock_name", s.get("stock_name", ""))
        s.setdefault("confidence", 0.8)
    stocks_7 = [{"stock_code": s.get("stock_code", ""), "stock_name": s.get("stock_name", ""), "price": float(s.get("price", 0)), "confidence": float(s.get("confidence", 0)), "strategy": "7根K线策略"} for s in signals[:10]]
    result = [
        {**STRATEGY_META[0], "stocks": stocks_7},
        {**STRATEGY_META[1], "stocks": []},
        {**STRATEGY_META[2], "stocks": []},
    ]
    return {"code": 200, "message": "success", "data": {"strategies": result}}

  contents: /**
 * 上帝之眼 - 首页（各策略推荐股票 + 存客宝风格内容区块）
 */
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import dynamic from 'next/dynamic'
import Link from 'next/link'
import { dataApi } from '@/lib/api'
import { APP_VERSION } from '@/lib/config'
import GlassCard from './components/ui/GlassCard'
import SectionHeader from './components/ui/SectionHeader'
import PriceChange from './components/ui/PriceChange'

const MiniTrendChart = dynamic(() => import('./components/ui/MiniTrendChart'), { ssr: false })

type StrategyItem = {
  id: string
  name: string
  description: string
  tag?: string
  stocks: Array<{ stock_code: string; stock_name: string; price: number; confidence?: number }>
}

export default function Home() {
  const [stats, setStats] = useState({ signals: 12, experts: 50, stocks: 1000 })
  const [signals, setSignals] = useState<any[]>([])
  const [strategies, setStrategies] = useState<StrategyItem[]>([])
  const [news, setNews] = useState<any[]>([])
  const [hotTopics, setHotTopics] = useState<{ code: string; mentions: number }[]>([])

  useEffect(() => {
    dataApi.signals(10).then((res) => {
      const items = res.data?.items || []
      setSignals(items.slice(0, 3))
    }).catch(() => {})
  }, [])

  useEffect(() => {
    dataApi.strategyRecommendations().then((res) => {
      const list = res.data?.strategies || []
      setStrategies(list)
    }).catch(() => {})
  }, [])

  useEffect(() => {
    fetch(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL || 'http://localhost:8000'}/api/v1/news/home?news_limit=15&topics_limit=10`)
      .then((r) => r.json())
      .then((data) => {
        const d = data.data || {}
        setNews(d.news || [])
        setHotTopics(d.hot_topics || [])
      })
      .catch(() => {})
  }, [])

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen">
      {/* 存客宝风格：顶栏白/浅底、标题清晰 */}
      <header className="glass-card-strong border-0 border-b border-white/10 rounded-b-2xl sticky top-0 z-40">
        <div className="px-4 py-3 flex items-center justify-between">
          <h1 className="text-lg font-bold text-white">上帝之眼</h1>
          <div className="flex gap-4 text-sm">
            <Link href="/" className="text-white font-medium">首页</Link>
            <Link href="/signals" className="text-white/60 hover:text-white">信号策略</Link>
          </div>
        </div>
      </header>

      <div className="px-4 py-4 space-y-6">
        {/* 标题区 - 存客宝式留白与层级 */}
        <div className="text-center pt-1">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white mb-1">AI驱动的量化交易系统</h2>
          <p className="text-sm text-white/70">基于卡若10年实战经验，融合最新AI技术</p>
        </div>

        <GlassCard className="overflow-hidden">
          <div className="video-config-wrap w-full bg-black/30 flex items-center justify-center">
            <div className="text-center text-white/60 text-sm px-4">
              <span className="text-3xl block mb-2">📺</span>
              视频配置
              <br />
              <span className="text-xs">直播/教程（固定比例，不扩展）</span>
            </div>
          </div>
        </GlassCard>

        {hotTopics.length > 0 && (
          <section>
            <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-white/80 mb-2">热点</h3>
            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
              {hotTopics.slice(0, 10).map((t: any) => (
                <Link
                  key={t.code}
                  href={`/stocks?code=${t.code}`}
                  className="glass-card rounded-xl px-4 py-2 text-sm text-white/90 hover:bg-white/20 transition"
                >
                  {t.code} <span className="text-white/50">({t.mentions})</span>
                </Link>
              ))}
            </div>
          </section>
        )}

        {news.length > 0 && (
          <section>
            <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-white/80 mb-2">新闻舆情</h3>
            <div className="space-y-3">
              {news.slice(0, 8).map((item: any) => (
                <a
                  key={item.post_id}
                  href={item.url || '#'}
                  target="_blank"
                  rel="noopener noreferrer"
                  className="glass-card rounded-xl p-4 block hover:bg-white/20 transition"
                >
                  <div className="font-medium text-white line-clamp-2">{item.title}</div>
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mt-2 text-white/60 text-xs">
                    <span>{item.platform}</span>
                    <span>{item.author_name}</span>
                    <span>👍 {item.likes}</span>
                    {item.stocks_mentioned?.length > 0 && (
                      <span>📈 {item.stocks_mentioned.slice(0, 3).join(' ')}</span>
                    )}
                  </div>
                </a>
              ))}
            </div>
          </section>
        )}

        <GlassCard className="overflow-hidden">
          <div className="px-3 pt-3 text-white/70 text-xs">近一周资产走势</div>
          <MiniTrendChart />
        </GlassCard>

        {/* 存客宝风格：三宫格数据卡片 */}
        <section className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-3">
          <GlassCard className="p-4 text-center">
            <span className="text-xs text-white/60 block mb-1">今日信号</span>
            <span className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">{stats.signals}</span>
            <span className="text-godeye-up text-xs block mt-1">+3 新增</span>
          </GlassCard>
          <GlassCard className="p-4 text-center">
            <span className="text-xs text-white/60 block mb-1">高手数量</span>
            <span className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">{stats.experts}</span>
            <span className="text-godeye-primary text-xs block mt-1">Top 50</span>
          </GlassCard>
          <GlassCard className="p-4 text-center">
            <span className="text-xs text-white/60 block mb-1">监控股票</span>
            <span className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">{stats.stocks}</span>
            <span className="text-godeye-green text-xs block mt-1">实时更新</span>
          </GlassCard>
        </section>

        {/* 各策略推荐股票 - 存客宝式卡片：每策略一卡，内为推荐股票列表 */}
        <section>
          <h3 className="text-base font-bold text-white mb-3 flex items-center gap-2">
            <span>🎯</span> 各策略推荐
          </h3>
          <div className="space-y-4">
            {strategies.length > 0 ? (
              strategies.map((s) => (
                <GlassCard key={s.id} className="p-4">
                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
                    <div>
                      <div className="font-semibold text-white">{s.name}</div>
                      <div className="text-white/60 text-sm mt-0.5">{s.description}</div>
                      {s.tag && (
                        <span className="inline-block mt-2 text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded bg-godeye-primary/20 text-godeye-primary">
                          {s.tag}
                        </span>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <div className="space-y-2">
                    {s.stocks.length > 0 ? (
                      s.stocks.map((stock) => (
                        <Link
                          key={stock.stock_code}
                          href={`/stocks?code=${stock.stock_code}`}
                          className="flex items-center justify-between py-2 px-3 rounded-lg bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 transition"
                        >
                          <div>
                            <div className="font-medium text-white text-sm">{stock.stock_name}</div>
                            <div className="text-white/50 text-xs">{stock.stock_code}</div>
                          </div>
                          <div className="text-right">
                            <div className="text-white font-medium text-sm">¥{Number(stock.price).toFixed(2)}</div>
                            {stock.confidence != null && (
                              <PriceChange value={Number((stock.confidence * 100).toFixed(1))} className="text-xs" />
                            )}
                          </div>
                        </Link>
                      ))
                    ) : (
                      <div className="py-3 text-center text-white/50 text-sm">暂无推荐</div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                </GlassCard>
              ))
            ) : (
              <GlassCard className="p-6 text-center text-white/50 text-sm">加载中...</GlassCard>
            )}
          </div>
        </section>

        <section>
          <h3 className="text-base font-bold text-white mb-3 flex items-center gap-2">
            <span>📡</span> 最新信号
          </h3>
          <div className="space-y-3">
            {signals.length > 0 ? (
              signals.map((signal: any, idx) => (
                <GlassCard key={idx} className="p-4 flex items-center justify-between">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                    <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-godeye-down/20 flex items-center justify-center text-lg border border-godeye-down/30">
                      🟢
                    </div>
                    <div>
                      <div className="font-semibold text-white">{signal.stock_name}</div>
                      <div className="text-white/60 text-xs">{signal.stock_code}</div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-right">
                    <div className="font-bold text-white">¥{signal.price?.toFixed(2)}</div>
                    <PriceChange value={(signal.confidence * 100) | 0} className="text-xs" />
                  </div>
                </GlassCard>
              ))
            ) : (
              <GlassCard className="p-6 text-center text-white/50 text-sm">

          </h3>

import Link from 'next/link'
import { ReactNode } from 'react'

type Props = {
  title: string
  moreHref?: string
  moreLabel?: string
  children: ReactNode
  className?: string
}

export default function Section({ title, moreHref, moreLabel = '更多', children, className = '' }: Props) {
  return (
    <section className={className}>
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
        <h3 className="text-base font-bold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">{title}</h3>

}

  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/3、自营项目/上帝之眼/frontend/app/components/StrategyStrip.tsx
  contents: /**
 * 智能体/策略横向滚动条 - 参考图：圆形图标 + 名称 + 推荐/AI 标签
 */
'use client'

import Link from 'next/link'

export type StrategyItem = {
  id: string
  name: string
  tag?: '推荐' | 'AI'
  href?: string
  icon?: string
  color?: string
}

const defaultColors = ['bg-godeye-primary/15 text-godeye-primary', 'bg-godeye-green/20 text-godeye-down', 'bg-godeye-gold/20 text-godeye-gold', 'bg-godeye-accent/15 text-godeye-accent']

export default function StrategyStrip({ items }: { items: StrategyItem[] }) {
  return (
    <div className="overflow-x-auto -mx-4 px-4 pb-1 scrollbar-hide">
      <div className="flex gap-4 min-w-max">
        {items.map((item, i) => {
          const color = item.color || defaultColors[i % defaultColors.length]
          const content = (
            <div className="flex flex-col items-center w-16 flex-shrink-0">
              <div className="relative">
                <div
                  className={`w-14 h-14 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center text-2xl ${color} border border-white shadow-sm`}
                >
                  {item.icon || '📊'}
                </div>
                {item.tag && (
                  <span
                    className={`absolute -top-0.5 -right-0.5 text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded ${
                      item.tag === 'AI' ? 'bg-godeye-accent text-white' : 'bg-godeye-gold text-white'
                    }`}
                  >
                    {item.tag}
                  </span>
                )}
              </div>
              <span className="mt-2 text-xs text-[var(--godeye-text-secondary)] text-center truncate w-full">
                {item.name}
              </span>
            </div>
          )}
          if (item.href) {
            return <Link key={item.id} href={item.href} className="flex-shrink-0">{content}</Link>
          }
          return <div key={item.id} className="flex-shrink-0">{content}</div>
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/3、自营项目/上帝之眼/frontend/app/components/AIChatBar.tsx
  contents: /**
 * AI 对话入口条 - 参考图底部：圆角输入框 + 语音/加号/相机图标
 */
'use client'

import { useState } from 'react'

type Props = {
  placeholder?: string
  onSend?: (text: string) => void
  onVoice?: () => void
  className?: string
}

export default function AIChatBar({
  placeholder = '有什么想问天眸的吗',
  onSend,
  onVoice,
  className = '',
}: Props) {
  const [value, setValue] = useState('')

  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault()
    const v = value.trim()
    if (v) {
      onSend?.(v)
      setValue('')
    }
  }

  return (
    <div
      className={`fixed left-0 right-0 bottom-0 z-40 max-w-lg mx-auto px-4 pb-2 safe-area-bottom ${className}`}
      style={{ paddingBottom: 'calc(3.5rem + 0.5rem + env(safe-area-inset-bottom, 0px))' }}
    >
      <form
        onSubmit={handleSubmit}
        className="card flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-3 rounded-2xl shadow-lg border border-black/5"
      >
        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={onVoice}
          className="flex-shrink-0 w-9 h-9 flex items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-[var(--godeye-bg)] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]"
          aria-label="语音"
        >
          <span className="text-lg">🎤</span>
        </button>
        <input
          type="text"
          value={value}
          onChange={(e) => setValue(e.target.value)}
          placeholder={placeholder}
          className="flex-1 min-w-0 py-2 bg-transparent text-[var(--godeye-text)] placeholder:text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-sm outline-none"
        />
        <button
          type="button"
          className="flex-shrink-0 w-9 h-9 flex items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-[var(--godeye-bg)] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]"
          aria-label="更多"
        >
          <span className="text-lg">➕</span>
        </button>
        <button
          type="submit"
          className="flex-shrink-0 w-9 h-9 flex items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-godeye-primary text-white"
          aria-label="发送"
        >
          <span className="text-lg">➤</span>
        </button>
      </form>
    </div>
  )
}

                          key={stock.stock_code}
                          href={`/stocks?code=${stock.stock_code}`}
                          className="flex items-center justify-between py-2 px-3 rounded-xl bg-[var(--godeye-bg)] hover:bg-black/5 transition"
                        >
                          <div>
                            <div className="font-medium text-[var(--godeye-text)] text-sm">{stock.stock_name}</div>
                            <div className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-xs">{stock.stock_code}</div>
                          </div>
                          <div className="text-right">
                            <div className="font-medium text-[var(--godeye-text)] text-sm">¥{Number(stock.price).toFixed(2)}</div>
                            {stock.confidence != null && (
                              <PriceChange value={Number((stock.confidence * 100).toFixed(1))} className="text-xs" />
                            )}
                          </div>
                        </Link>
                      ))
                    ) : (
                      <div className="py-3 text-center text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-sm">暂无推荐</div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                </Card>
              ))
            ) : (
              <Card className="p-6 text-center text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-sm">加载中...</Card>
            )}
          </div>
        </Section>

        {/* 热点 */}
        {hotTopics.length > 0 && (
          <Section title="热点">
            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
              {hotTopics.slice(0, 10).map((t: any) => (
                <Link
                  key={t.code}
                  href={`/stocks?code=${t.code}`}
                  className="card px-4 py-2 text-sm text-[var(--godeye-text)] hover:bg-black/5 transition inline-block"
                >
                  {t.code} <span className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">({t.mentions})</span>
                </Link>
              ))}
            </div>
          </Section>
        )}

        {/* 新闻舆情 */}
        {news.length > 0 && (
          <Section title="新闻舆情" moreHref="#">
            <div className="space-y-3">
              {news.slice(0, 5).map((item: any) => (
                <a
                  key={item.post_id}
                  href={item.url || '#'}
                  target="_blank"
                  rel="noopener noreferrer"
                  className="card p-4 block hover:bg-black/5 transition"
                >
                  <div className="font-medium text-[var(--godeye-text)] line-clamp-2">{item.title}</div>
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mt-2 text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-xs">
                    <span>{item.platform}</span>
                    <span>👍 {item.likes}</span>
                  </div>
                </a>
              ))}
            </div>
          </Section>
        )}

        {/* 资产走势 */}
        <Card className="overflow-hidden p-4">
          <div className="text-[var(--godeye-text-secondary)] text-xs mb-2">近一周资产走势</div>
          <MiniTrendChart />
        </Card>

        {/* 最新信号 */}
        <Section title="最新信号" moreHref="/signals">
          <div className="space-y-3">
            {signals.length > 0 ? (
              signals.map((signal: any, idx) => (
                <Card key={idx} className="p-4 flex items-center justify-between">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                    <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-godeye-down/15 flex items-center justify-center text-lg border border-godeye-down/30">
                      🟢
                    </div>
                    <div>
                      <div className="font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">{signal.stock_name}</div>
                      <div className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-xs">{signal.stock_code}</div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-right">
                    <div className="font-bold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">¥{signal.price?.toFixed(2)}</div>
                    <PriceChange value={(signal.confidence * 100) | 0} className="text-xs" />
                  </div>
                </Card>
              ))
            ) : (
              <Card className="p-6 text-center text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-sm">暂无最新信号</Card>
            )}
          </div>
        </Section>

        {/* 核心策略说明 - 紧凑卡片 */}
        <Section title="核心策略说明">
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-3">
            <div className="card rounded-xl p-4 border border-godeye-down/20 bg-godeye-down/5">
              <div className="font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">7根K线策略</div>
              <div className="text-[var(--godeye-text-secondary)] text-sm mt-1">节假日前2天买入，第7天卖出</div>
              <div className="text-godeye-down text-xs mt-2">年化收益: 18.84%</div>
            </div>
            <div className="card rounded-xl p-4 border border-godeye-primary/20 bg-godeye-primary/5">
              <div className="font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">节假日强中强</div>
              <div className="text-[var(--godeye-text-secondary)] text-sm mt-1">强势板块中的强势个股</div>
              <div className="text-godeye-primary text-xs mt-2">胜率: 62.8%</div>
            </div>
            <div className="card rounded-xl p-4 border border-black/5">
              <div className="font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">高手跟踪</div>
              <div className="text-[var(--godeye-text-secondary)] text-sm mt-1">AI 实时监控前10名高手</div>
              <div className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-xs mt-2">延迟 &lt;1秒</div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </Section>

        <footer className="py-4 text-center text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-xs">
          上帝之眼 {APP_VERSION} · 基于卡若实战经验
        </footer>
      </div>

      {/* 仅首页展示 AI 对话入口条 */}
      <AIChatBar
        placeholder="有什么想问天眸的吗"
        onSend={(text) => console.log('AI send:', text)}
      />
    </div>
  )
}

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import { dataApi } from '@/lib/api'
import Card from '../components/ui/Card'

export default function SignalsPage() {

  useEffect(() => {
    dataApi.signals(50).then((res) => setSignals((res.data?.items || []).slice(0, 50))).catch(() => {})
  }, [])

  return (

      <header className="sticky top-0 z-40 bg-[var(--godeye-bg-elevated)] border-b border-black/5">

        </div>
      </header>

      <div className="px-4 py-4 space-y-4">
        <Card className="p-4 flex gap-3 flex-wrap">
          <select className="flex-1 min-w-0 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-sm bg-[var(--godeye-bg)] border border-black/8 text-[var(--godeye-text)]">
            <option>全部策略</option>

          <select className="flex-1 min-w-0 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-sm bg-[var(--godeye-bg)] border border-black/8 text-[var(--godeye-text)]">
            <option>全部类型</option>
            <option>买入</option>
            <option>卖出</option>
          </select>
        </Card>

        <div className="space-y-4">
          {signals.map((signal: any) => (
            <Card key={signal.signal_id} className="p-4">
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3">

                    🟢
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <h3 className="font-bold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">{signal.stock_name}</h3>
                    <p className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-sm">{signal.stock_code}</p>

                </span>

                  <div className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-xs">信号价</div>

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/3、自营项目/上帝之眼/frontend/app/stocks/page.tsx
  contents: /**
 * 股票监控 - 浅色卡片风格
 */
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import { dataApi, meApi } from '@/lib/api'
import Card from '../components/ui/Card'
import PriceChange from '../components/ui/PriceChange'

export default function StocksPage() {
  const [stocks, setStocks] = useState<any[]>([])
  const [watchlistCodes, setWatchlistCodes] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set())
  const [adding, setAdding] = useState<string | null>(null)

  useEffect(() => {
    dataApi.stocks(50).then((res) => setStocks((res.data || []).slice(0, 50))).catch(() => {})
    meApi.watchlist().then((res) => setWatchlistCodes(new Set((res.data || []).map((x) => x.code)))).catch(() => {})
  }, [])

  const addToWatchlist = async (code: string, name: string) => {
    setAdding(code)
    try {
      await meApi.addWatchlist(code, name)
      setWatchlistCodes((prev) => new Set([...prev, code]))
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e)
    } finally {
      setAdding(null)
    }
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-[var(--godeye-bg)]">
      <header className="sticky top-0 z-40 bg-[var(--godeye-bg-elevated)] border-b border-black/5">
        <div className="px-4 py-3">
          <h1 className="text-lg font-bold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">📈 股票监控</h1>
          <p className="text-xs text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] mt-0.5">自选与行情</p>
        </div>
      </header>

      <div className="px-4 py-4 space-y-3">
        {stocks.map((stock: any) => {
          const inWatch = watchlistCodes.has(stock.code)
          return (
            <Card key={stock.code} className="p-4 flex items-center justify-between gap-3">
              <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
                <h3 className="font-bold text-[var(--godeye-text)] truncate">{stock.name}</h3>
                <p className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-sm">{stock.code}</p>
                <p className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-xs mt-1">{stock.sector}</p>
              </div>
              <div className="text-right flex-shrink-0 flex items-center gap-2">
                <div>
                  <div className="text-lg font-bold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">¥{stock.price?.toFixed(2)}</div>
                  <PriceChange value={(stock.change_pct * 100)} className="text-sm font-medium" />
                </div>
                {!inWatch && (
                  <button
                    onClick={() => addToWatchlist(stock.code, stock.name)}
                    disabled={adding === stock.code}
                    className="rounded-xl px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium bg-godeye-primary/15 text-godeye-primary border border-godeye-primary/30"
                  >
                    {adding === stock.code ? '...' : '加自选'}
                  </button>
                )}
                {inWatch && <span className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-xs">已选</span>}
              </div>
            </Card>
          )
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

                <div className="font-bold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">{(expert.win_rate * 100).toFixed(1)}%</div>
                <div className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-xs">胜率</div>
              </div>
              <div className="rounded-xl py-2 bg-[var(--godeye-bg)]">
                <div className="text-godeye-primary font-bold">{expert.sharpe_ratio?.toFixed(2)}</div>
                <div className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-xs">夏普</div>
              </div>
            </div>
            <button className="w-full rounded-xl py-2.5 text-sm font-bold text-white bg-godeye-primary hover:opacity-90">
              + 关注高手
            </button>
          </Card>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

已按你提供的参考图风格（不参考具体内容）完成前端架构与 AI 入口调整，构建通过。变更总结如下：

---

**一、整体风格（对齐阿福/智能体/运动健康小助手）**

- **浅色主题**：背景改为 `#f5f6f8`，内容区白底卡片，替代原深色毛玻璃。
- **圆角与阴影**：统一使用 `--godeye-card-radius`、`--godeye-card-shadow`，卡片白底、轻阴影。
- **层级与留白**：区块标题 + 可选「更多 >」，段落和卡片间距加大。

**二、新增/调整的组件**

| 组件 | 作用 |
|------|------|
| `Card` | 通用白底圆角卡片，替代原玻璃卡片的展示场景。 |
| `Section` | 区块容器：标题 + 可选「更多」链接。 |
| `StrategyStrip` | **智能体**横向滚动：圆形图标 + 名称 + 「推荐」/「AI」小标签，可点进策略/信号。 |
| `AIChatBar` | **AI 对话入口**：底部固定圆角输入条（占位「有什么想问天眸的吗」）+ 语音 / 更多 / 发送，仅首页展示、位于底部导航上方。 |

**三、页面与布局**

- **首页**：顶栏（菜单 + 标题 + 信号/设置图标）→ 问候 → 三宫格数据卡 → **智能体**横向条（7根K线、节假日强中强、高手跟踪、网红流量）→ 各策略推荐 → 热点 / 新闻 / 资产走势 / 最新信号 / 核心策略说明 → 底部 **AI 输入条**。
- **信号 / 股票 / 高手 / 设置（含绑定账户）**：统一为浅色背景 + `Card` + `text-[var(--godeye-text)]` 等变量，与首页一致。
- **底部导航**：白底、顶部分割线、选中项用主色，风格与参考图一致。

**四、设计令牌（`globals.css`）**

- 新增/沿用：`--godeye-bg`、`--godeye-bg-elevated`、`--godeye-card-bg`、`--godeye-card-shadow`、`--godeye-accent`、`--godeye-text` / `-secondary` / `-muted`，便于全站统一和后续扩展。

**五、AI 功能入口**

- 首页底部固定 **AIChatBar**：输入框 + 发送（当前 `onSend` 仅 `console.log`，可后续接天眸对话 API）。
- 智能体区提供策略/功能入口，用「推荐」「AI」标签区分，便于扩展更多策略或 AI 能力。

本地可执行：在 `frontend` 目录运行 `npm run dev`，浏览器打开 `http://localhost:3006` 查看新首页与各页浅色风格及 AI 入口。若需要把「问天眸」接到真实对话接口或加语音/多模态，可以再说具体需求。

    """初始化数据库连接。主库仅 MySQL（Docker）；Redis 可选。失败时仅告警不阻塞启动。"""
    global mongo_client, redis_client, mysql_pool

    # MySQL（唯一主库，Docker 内）
    use_mysql = getattr(settings, "USE_MYSQL_AS_PRIMARY", True)

- 前端：在 `frontend` 目录执行 `npm run dev`，已用该方式在后台启动，监听 **3006**。
