 * 上帝之眼 - 首页（手机界面、蚂蚁阿福风格、极简）
 */
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import Link from 'next/link'
import { dataApi } from '@/lib/api'
import Card from './components/ui/Card'
import PriceChange from './components/ui/PriceChange'
import StrategyStrip from './components/StrategyStrip'
import AIChatBar from './components/AIChatBar'
import type { StrategyItem } from './components/StrategyStrip'

type StrategyDetail = {
  id: string
  name: string
  description: string
  tag?: string
  stocks: Array<{ stock_code: string; stock_name: string; price: number; confidence?: number }>
}

export default function Home() {
  const [stats] = useState({ signals: 12, experts: 50, stocks: 1000 })
  const [signals, setSignals] = useState<any[]>([])
  const [strategies, setStrategies] = useState<StrategyDetail[]>([])

  useEffect(() => {
    dataApi.signals(10).then((res) => {
      setSignals((res.data?.items || []).slice(0, 3))
    }).catch(() => {})
  }, [])
  useEffect(() => {
    dataApi.strategyRecommendations().then((res) => {
      setStrategies(res.data?.strategies || [])
    }).catch(() => {})
  }, [])

  const stripItems: StrategyItem[] = [
    { id: '7k', name: '7根K线', tag: '推荐', icon: '📐', href: '/signals' },
    { id: 'holiday', name: '节假日', tag: 'AI', icon: '🎯', href: '/signals' },
    { id: 'expert', name: '高手', tag: 'AI', icon: '👥', href: '/experts' },
  ]

  const firstStrategy = strategies[0]

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen pb-20">
      {/* 顶栏：紧凑、阿福式 */}
      <header className="sticky top-0 z-40 bg-[var(--godeye-bg-elevated)] border-b border-black/[0.06] safe-area-top">
        <div className="px-4 h-12 flex items-center justify-between">
          <h1 className="text-base font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">上帝之眼</h1>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
            <Link href="/signals" className="p-2 rounded-full active:bg-black/5" aria-label="信号">📡</Link>
            <Link href="/settings" className="p-2 rounded-full active:bg-black/5" aria-label="我的">⚙️</Link>
          </div>
        </div>
      </header>

      <div className="px-4 pt-4 pb-6 space-y-5">
        {/* 问候：一行 */}
        <p className="text-[var(--godeye-text-secondary)] text-sm">让每个信号都值得参考</p>

        {/* 三宫格：小卡片 */}
        <section className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2">
          <Card className="p-3 text-center rounded-xl">
            <div className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] uppercase tracking-wide">信号</div>
            <div className="text-lg font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)] mt-0.5">{stats.signals}</div>
          </Card>
          <Card className="p-3 text-center rounded-xl">
            <div className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] uppercase tracking-wide">高手</div>
            <div className="text-lg font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)] mt-0.5">{stats.experts}</div>
          </Card>
          <Card className="p-3 text-center rounded-xl">
            <div className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] uppercase tracking-wide">股票</div>
            <div className="text-lg font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)] mt-0.5">{stats.stocks}</div>
          </Card>
        </section>

        {/* 智能体入口：横向圆点 */}
        <div>
          <div className="text-xs font-medium text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] mb-2">智能体</div>
          <StrategyStrip items={stripItems} />
        </div>

        {/* 策略推荐：只展示第一个策略，一张卡 */}
        <div>
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
            <span className="text-xs font-medium text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">策略推荐</span>
            <Link href="/signals" className="text-xs text-godeye-primary">更多</Link>
          </div>
          <Card className="rounded-xl p-4">
            {firstStrategy ? (
              <>
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
                  <span className="font-medium text-[var(--godeye-text)] text-sm">{firstStrategy.name}</span>
                  {firstStrategy.tag && (
                    <span className="text-[10px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full bg-godeye-primary/10 text-godeye-primary">
                      {firstStrategy.tag}
                    </span>
                  )}
                </div>
                {firstStrategy.stocks.length > 0 ? (
                  <div className="space-y-2">
                    {firstStrategy.stocks.slice(0, 5).map((s) => (
                      <Link
                        key={s.stock_code}
                        href={`/stocks?code=${s.stock_code}`}
                        className="flex items-center justify-between py-2 border-t border-black/5 first:border-0"
                      >
                        <span className="text-sm text-[var(--godeye-text)]">{s.stock_name}</span>
                        <span className="text-sm font-medium text-[var(--godeye-text)]">¥{Number(s.price).toFixed(2)}</span>
                      </Link>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                ) : (
                  <p className="text-xs text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] py-2">暂无推荐</p>
                )}
              </>
            ) : (
              <p className="text-xs text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] py-2">加载中...</p>
            )}
          </Card>
        </div>

        {/* 最新信号：3 条列表 */}
        <div>
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
            <span className="text-xs font-medium text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">最新信号</span>
            <Link href="/signals" className="text-xs text-godeye-primary">更多</Link>
          </div>
          <Card className="rounded-xl overflow-hidden">
            {signals.length > 0 ? (
              signals.map((s: any, i: number) => (
                <Link
                  key={i}
                  href={`/stocks?code=${s.stock_code}`}
                  className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-black/5 last:border-0 active:bg-black/5"
                >
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                    <span className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-godeye-down/15 flex items-center justify-center text-sm">🟢</span>
                    <div>
                      <div className="text-sm font-medium text-[var(--godeye-text)]">{s.stock_name}</div>
                      <div className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">{s.stock_code}</div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-right">
                    <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">¥{s.price?.toFixed(2)}</div>
                    <PriceChange value={(s.confidence * 100) | 0} className="text-[10px]" />
                  </div>
                </Link>
              ))
            ) : (
              <div className="px-4 py-6 text-center text-xs text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">暂无信号</div>
            )}
          </Card>
        </div>
      </div>

      <AIChatBar placeholder="有什么想问天眸的吗" onSend={(t) => console.log(t)} />
    </div>
  )
}

已按「手机界面 + 蚂蚁阿福风格 + 更简单」做完重构，构建通过。变更总结如下：

---

**1. 界面尺寸与手机约束**

- **主内容区**：`max-w-[428px]` 居中，模拟常见手机宽度，大屏上像单栏手机框。
- **底部导航 & AI 输入条**：同宽 `max-w-[428px]`，与主内容对齐。
- **viewport**：`width: device-width`、`viewportFit: cover`，适配刘海/安全区。

**2. 风格（对齐蚂蚁阿福）**

- **背景**：浅灰白 `#f7f8fa`，顶栏与卡片为白 `#ffffff`。
- **卡片**：圆角 `12px`、轻阴影、统一 `rounded-xl`。
- **字体**：正文约 15px，区块标题为小号次要色，信息层级更清晰。
- **顶栏**：单行标题 + 右侧图标，高度约 `h-12`，更紧凑。
- **底部导航**：高度 `h-12`，图标 + 小字标签，选中用主色。

**3. 首页结构精简**

- **保留**：顶栏 → 一句 slogan → 三宫格（信号/高手/股票）→ 智能体横向圆点 → **一张**策略推荐卡（只展示第一个策略）→ 最新信号（3 条列表）→ AI 输入条。
- **移除**：热点、新闻舆情、资产走势、核心策略说明、页脚版本号，减少区块和滚动长度。
- **策略推荐**：从「多策略多卡」改为「一个策略一张卡」，最多 5 只股票，带「更多」跳转信号页。
- **最新信号**：列表式，每行名称 + 代码 + 价格 + 置信度，可点进股票。

**4. 组件与全局**

- **StrategyStrip**：圆形缩小为 `w-11 h-11`，间距 `gap-3`，更适配小屏。
- **globals**：增加 `--godeye-page-px`（预留）、`safe-area-top`，卡片圆角与阴影统一。
- **AIChatBar**：底部位置按 `h-12` 导航条高度微调。

在浏览器打开 **http://localhost:3006** 即可看到：单栏手机宽度、浅色卡片、少量区块和底部 AI 条，整体更接近蚂蚁阿福的简洁手机界面。

'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import Link from 'next/link'
import { dataApi } from '@/lib/api'
import Card from './components/ui/Card'
import PriceChange from './components/ui/PriceChange'
import StrategyStrip from './components/StrategyStrip'
import AIChatBar from './components/AIChatBar'
import type { StrategyItem } from './components/StrategyStrip'

type StrategyDetail = {
  id: string
  name: string
  description: string
  tag?: string
  stocks: Array<{ stock_code: string; stock_name: string; price: number; confidence?: number }>
}

export default function Home() {
  const [stats] = useState({ signals: 12, experts: 50, stocks: 1000 })
  const [signals, setSignals] = useState<any[]>([])
  const [strategies, setStrategies] = useState<StrategyDetail[]>([])

  useEffect(() => {
    dataApi.signals(10).then((res) => setSignals((res.data?.items || []).slice(0, 3))).catch(() => {})
  }, [])
  useEffect(() => {
    dataApi.strategyRecommendations().then((res) => setStrategies(res.data?.strategies || [])).catch(() => {})
  }, [])

  const stripItems: StrategyItem[] = [
    { id: '7k', name: '7根K线', tag: '推荐', icon: '📐', href: '/signals' },
    { id: 'holiday', name: '节假日', tag: 'AI', icon: '🎯', href: '/signals' },
    { id: 'expert', name: '高手', tag: 'AI', icon: '👥', href: '/experts' },
  ]

  const firstStrategy = strategies[0]

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen pb-24">
      {/* 顶栏：截图风格 - 左上头像+名称+订单·设置，右上消息+任务中心 */}
      <header className="sticky top-0 z-40 bg-[var(--godeye-bg-elevated)] border-b border-black/[0.06] safe-area-top">
        <div className="px-4 py-3 flex items-center justify-between">
          <Link href="/settings" className="flex items-center gap-3 min-w-0 flex-1">
            <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-godeye-primary/15 flex items-center justify-center text-godeye-primary flex-shrink-0 text-lg">
              👁
            </div>
            <div className="min-w-0">
              <div className="font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)] truncate">上帝之眼</div>
              <div className="text-xs text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">订单·设置 &gt;</div>
            </div>
          </Link>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-1 flex-shrink-0">
            <Link href="/signals" className="flex flex-col items-center p-2 rounded-lg active:bg-black/5" aria-label="消息">
              <span className="text-lg">🔔</span>
              <span className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">消息</span>
            </Link>
            <Link href="/experts" className="flex flex-col items-center p-2 rounded-lg active:bg-black/5" aria-label="任务中心">
              <span className="text-lg">🎁</span>
              <span className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">任务中心</span>
            </Link>
          </div>
        </div>
      </header>

      <div className="px-4 pt-4 pb-6 space-y-5">
        {/* 双主卡：医疗保障/健康档案 风格 -> 策略信号 / 股票监控 */}
        <section className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
          <Link href="/signals" className="card rounded-xl p-4 flex items-center gap-3 active:bg-black/5">
            <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-full bg-godeye-primary/15 flex items-center justify-center text-xl flex-shrink-0 text-godeye-primary">
              📡
            </div>
            <div className="min-w-0">
              <div className="font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)] text-sm">策略信号</div>
              <div className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] mt-0.5">7根K线·高手跟单</div>
            </div>
          </Link>
          <Link href="/stocks" className="card rounded-xl p-4 flex items-center gap-3 active:bg-black/5">
            <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-full bg-godeye-accent/15 flex items-center justify-center text-xl flex-shrink-0 text-godeye-accent">
              📈
            </div>
            <div className="min-w-0">
              <div className="font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)] text-sm">股票监控</div>
              <div className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] mt-0.5">自选·行情</div>
            </div>
          </Link>
        </section>

        {/* 智能体：标题 + 更多 > + 横向滚动 */}
        <section>
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
            <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">智能体</span>
            <Link href="/signals" className="text-xs text-godeye-primary">更多 &gt;</Link>
          </div>
          <StrategyStrip items={stripItems} />
        </section>

        {/* 策略推荐：一张卡 */}
        <section>
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
            <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">策略推荐</span>
            <Link href="/signals" className="text-xs text-godeye-primary">更多 &gt;</Link>
          </div>
          <Card className="rounded-xl p-4">
            {firstStrategy ? (
              <>
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
                  <span className="font-medium text-[var(--godeye-text)] text-sm">{firstStrategy.name}</span>
                  {firstStrategy.tag && (
                    <span className="text-[10px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full bg-godeye-primary/10 text-godeye-primary">
                      {firstStrategy.tag}
                    </span>
                  )}
                </div>
                {firstStrategy.stocks.length > 0 ? (
                  <div className="space-y-2">
                    {firstStrategy.stocks.slice(0, 5).map((s) => (
                      <Link
                        key={s.stock_code}
                        href={`/stocks?code=${s.stock_code}`}
                        className="flex items-center justify-between py-2 border-t border-black/5 first:border-0 active:bg-black/5"
                      >
                        <span className="text-sm text-[var(--godeye-text)]">{s.stock_name}</span>
                        <span className="text-sm font-medium text-[var(--godeye-text)]">¥{Number(s.price).toFixed(2)}</span>
                      </Link>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                ) : (
                  <p className="text-xs text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] py-2">暂无推荐</p>
                )}
              </>
            ) : (
              <p className="text-xs text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] py-2">加载中...</p>
            )}
          </Card>
        </section>

        {/* 最近信号：对话记录风格，列表+日期 */}
        <section>
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
            <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">最近信号</span>
            <Link href="/signals" className="text-xs text-godeye-primary">更多 &gt;</Link>
          </div>
          <Card className="rounded-xl overflow-hidden">
            {signals.length > 0 ? (
              <div className="divide-y divide-black/5">
                {signals.map((s: any, i: number) => (
                  <Link
                    key={i}
                    href={`/stocks?code=${s.stock_code}`}
                    className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 active:bg-black/5"
                  >
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-3 min-w-0">
                      <span className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-godeye-down/15 flex items-center justify-center text-sm flex-shrink-0">🟢</span>
                      <div className="min-w-0">
                        <div className="text-sm font-medium text-[var(--godeye-text)] truncate">{s.stock_name}</div>
                        <div className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">{s.stock_code}</div>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <div className="text-right flex-shrink-0 ml-2">
                      <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">¥{s.price?.toFixed(2)}</div>
                      <PriceChange value={(s.confidence * 100) | 0} className="text-[10px]" />
                    </div>
                  </Link>
                ))}
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div className="px-4 py-6 text-center text-xs text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">暂无信号</div>
            )}
          </Card>
        </section>

        {/* 底部快捷入口：阿福式 4 个圆角按钮 */}
        <section className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 pt-2">
          <Link href="/signals?strategy=7k" className="card rounded-xl py-3 flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-1 active:bg-black/5">
            <span className="text-lg">📐</span>
            <span className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-secondary)]">7根K线</span>
          </Link>
          <Link href="/signals?strategy=holiday" className="card rounded-xl py-3 flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-1 active:bg-black/5">
            <span className="text-lg">🎯</span>
            <span className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-secondary)]">节假日</span>
          </Link>
          <Link href="/experts" className="card rounded-xl py-3 flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-1 active:bg-black/5">
            <span className="text-lg">👥</span>
            <span className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-secondary)]">高手</span>
          </Link>
          <div className="card rounded-xl py-3 flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-1 bg-godeye-primary/10 border border-godeye-primary/20">
            <span className="text-lg">💬</span>
            <span className="text-[10px] text-godeye-primary">问天眸</span>
          </div>
        </section>
      </div>

      <AIChatBar placeholder="天眸能做什么" onSend={(t) => console.log(t)} />
    </div>
  )
}

  old_string: async function request<T>(path: string, options?: RequestInit): Promise<ApiRes<T>> {
  const url = path.startsWith('http') ? path : `${API_BASE}${path}`
  const res = await fetch(url, {
    ...options,
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', ...options?.headers },
  })
  const json = await res.json().catch(() => ({}))
  if (!res.ok) return { code: res.status, message: json?.message || res.statusText, data: json as T }
  return json as ApiRes<T>
}
  new_string: async function request<T>(path: string, options?: RequestInit): Promise<ApiRes<T>> {
  const url = path.startsWith('http') ? path : `${API_BASE}${path}`
  let res: Response
  try {
    res = await fetch(url, {
      ...options,
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', ...options?.headers },
    })
  } catch (e) {
    return { code: -1, message: '网络异常，请检查后端是否启动', data: undefined as T }
  }
  const json = await res.json().catch(() => ({}))
  if (!res.ok) return { code: res.status, message: json?.message || res.statusText, data: json as T }
  return json as ApiRes<T>
}

import Link from 'next/link'
import { dataApi } from '@/lib/api'
import Card from './components/ui/Card'
import PriceChange from './components/ui/PriceChange'
import StrategyStrip from './components/StrategyStrip'
import AIChatBar from './components/AIChatBar'
import type { StrategyItem } from './components/StrategyStrip'

type StrategyDetail = {
  id: string
  name: string
  description: string
  tag?: string
  stocks: Array<{ stock_code: string; stock_name: string; price: number; confidence?: number }>
}

const PROMPT_ITEMS = [
  { text: '节前该买什么？', href: '/signals' },
  { text: '高手持仓怎么看？', href: '/experts' },
  { text: '天眸能做什么？', href: '#' },
]

export default function Home() {
  const [stats] = useState({ signals: 12, experts: 50, stocks: 1000 })
  const [signals, setSignals] = useState<any[]>([])
  const [strategies, setStrategies] = useState<StrategyDetail[]>([])

  useEffect(() => {
    dataApi.signals(10).then((res) => setSignals((res.data?.items || []).slice(0, 3))).catch(() => {})
  }, [])
  useEffect(() => {
    dataApi.strategyRecommendations().then((res) => setStrategies(res.data?.strategies || [])).catch(() => {})
  }, [])

  const stripItems: StrategyItem[] = [
    { id: '7k', name: '7根K线', tag: '推荐', icon: '📐', href: '/signals' },

  ]

  const firstStrategy = strategies[0]
  const now = new Date()
  const updateStr = `更新于${now.getMonth() + 1}-${String(now.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')} ${String(now.getHours()).padStart(2, '0')}:${String(now.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0')}`

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen pb-24 bg-[var(--godeye-bg)]">
      {/* 顶栏：左汉堡+居中标题+右三图标，与参考图一致 */}

          <button type="button" className="p-2 -ml-2 rounded-lg active:bg-black/5" aria-label="菜单">
            <span className="text-[var(--godeye-text)]">☰</span>

          <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
            <Link href="/signals" className="p-2 rounded-lg active:bg-black/5" aria-label="信号">📡</Link>
            <Link href="/settings" className="p-2 rounded-lg active:bg-black/5" aria-label="设置">⚙️</Link>
            <button type="button" className="p-2 rounded-lg active:bg-black/5" aria-label="更多">⋯</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </header>

        {/* 问候区：哈喽 ✨ + 标语，与参考图一致 */}

                    <Link key={s.stock_code} href={`/stocks?code=${s.stock_code}`} className="flex items-center justify-between py-2 border-t border-black/5 first:border-0 active:bg-black/5">
                      <span className="text-sm text-[var(--godeye-text)]">{s.stock_name}</span>
                      <span className="text-sm font-medium text-[var(--godeye-text)]">¥{Number(s.price).toFixed(2)}</span>
                    </Link>
                  ))
                ) : (
                  <p className="text-xs text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] py-2">暂无推荐</p>
                )}
              </>
            ) : (
              <p className="text-xs text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] py-2">加载中...</p>
            )}
          </Card>
        </section>

        {/* 最近信号 */}
        <section>
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
            <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">最近信号</span>
            <Link href="/signals" className="text-xs text-godeye-primary">更多 &gt;</Link>
          </div>
          <Card className="rounded-2xl overflow-hidden">
            {signals.length > 0 ? (
              <div className="divide-y divide-black/5">
                {signals.map((s: any, i: number) => (
                  <Link key={i} href={`/stocks?code=${s.stock_code}`} className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 active:bg-black/5">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-3 min-w-0">
                      <span className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-godeye-down/15 flex items-center justify-center text-sm flex-shrink-0">🟢</span>
                      <div className="min-w-0">
                        <div className="text-sm font-medium text-[var(--godeye-text)] truncate">{s.stock_name}</div>
                        <div className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">{s.stock_code}</div>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <div className="text-right flex-shrink-0 ml-2">
                      <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">¥{s.price?.toFixed(2)}</div>
                      <PriceChange value={(s.confidence * 100) | 0} className="text-[10px]" />
                    </div>
                  </Link>
                ))}
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div className="px-4 py-6 text-center text-xs text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">暂无信号</div>
            )}
          </Card>
        </section>

        {/* 底部快捷：4 个圆角图标+文字，与参考图一致 */}
        <section className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 pt-2">
          <Link href="/signals?strategy=7k" className="card rounded-2xl py-4 flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-1.5 active:bg-black/5">
            <span className="text-xl">📐</span>
            <span className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-secondary)]">7根K线</span>
          </Link>
          <Link href="/signals?strategy=holiday" className="card rounded-2xl py-4 flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-1.5 active:bg-black/5">
            <span className="text-xl">🎯</span>
            <span className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-secondary)]">节假日</span>
          </Link>
          <Link href="/experts" className="card rounded-2xl py-4 flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-1.5 active:bg-black/5">
            <span className="text-xl">👥</span>
            <span className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-secondary)]">高手</span>
          </Link>
          <div className="card rounded-2xl py-4 flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-1.5 bg-gradient-to-br from-godeye-primary/10 to-godeye-accent/10 border border-godeye-primary/15">
            <span className="text-xl">💬</span>
            <span className="text-[10px] text-godeye-primary font-medium">问天眸</span>
          </div>
        </section>
      </div>

      <AIChatBar placeholder="天眸能做什么" onSend={(t) => console.log(t)} />
    </div>
  )
}

                </span>
              </div>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 text-sm mb-3">
                <div className="rounded-2xl p-3 bg-white/80">
                  <div className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-xs">信号价</div>
                  <div className="font-bold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">¥{signal.price?.toFixed(2) || '0.00'}</div>
                </div>
                <div className="rounded-2xl p-3 bg-white/80">
                  <div className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-xs">置信度</div>
                  <div className="font-bold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">{(signal.confidence * 100).toFixed(0)}%</div>
                </div>
              </div>
              <button className="w-full rounded-2xl py-3 text-sm font-bold text-white bg-godeye-primary hover:opacity-90">
                一键跟单
              </button>
            </Card>
          ))}

          {signals.length === 0 && (
            <Card className="rounded-2xl p-8 text-center">
              <div className="text-4xl mb-3">📭</div>
              <div className="font-medium text-[var(--godeye-text)] mb-1">暂无交易信号</div>
              <div className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-sm">系统正在分析市场，请稍候...</div>
            </Card>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/3、自营项目/上帝之眼/frontend/app/stocks/page.tsx
  contents: /**
 * 股票监控 - 阿福风格统一顶栏与卡片
 */
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import { dataApi, meApi } from '@/lib/api'
import Card from '../components/ui/Card'
import PriceChange from '../components/ui/PriceChange'
import AppHeader from '../components/AppHeader'

export default function StocksPage() {
  const [stocks, setStocks] = useState<any[]>([])
  const [watchlistCodes, setWatchlistCodes] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set())
  const [adding, setAdding] = useState<string | null>(null)

  useEffect(() => {
    dataApi.stocks(50).then((res) => setStocks((res.data || []).slice(0, 50))).catch(() => {})
    meApi.watchlist().then((res) => setWatchlistCodes(new Set((res.data || []).map((x) => x.code)))).catch(() => {})
  }, [])

  const addToWatchlist = async (code: string, name: string) => {
    setAdding(code)
    try {
      await meApi.addWatchlist(code, name)
      setWatchlistCodes((prev) => new Set([...prev, code]))
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e)
    } finally {
      setAdding(null)
    }
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-[var(--godeye-bg)]">
      <AppHeader title="股票监控" showBack backHref="/" />

      <div className="px-4 pt-4 pb-6 space-y-3">
        {stocks.map((stock: any) => {
          const inWatch = watchlistCodes.has(stock.code)
          return (
            <Card key={stock.code} className="rounded-2xl p-4 flex items-center justify-between gap-3">
              <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
                <h3 className="font-bold text-[var(--godeye-text)] truncate">{stock.name}</h3>
                <p className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-sm">{stock.code}</p>
                <p className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-xs mt-1">{stock.sector}</p>
              </div>
              <div className="text-right flex-shrink-0 flex items-center gap-2">
                <div>
                  <div className="text-lg font-bold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">¥{stock.price?.toFixed(2)}</div>
                  <PriceChange value={(stock.change_pct * 100)} className="text-sm font-medium" />
                </div>
                {!inWatch && (
                  <button
                    onClick={() => addToWatchlist(stock.code, stock.name)}
                    disabled={adding === stock.code}
                    className="rounded-2xl px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium bg-godeye-primary/15 text-godeye-primary border border-godeye-primary/30"
                  >
                    {adding === stock.code ? '...' : '加自选'}
                  </button>
                )}
                {inWatch && <span className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] text-xs">已选</span>}
              </div>
            </Card>
          )
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/3、自营项目/上帝之眼/frontend/app/settings/accounts/bind/page.tsx
  contents: /**
 * 绑定交易账户 - 阿福风格统一顶栏与卡片
 */
'use client'

import { useState } from 'react'
import Link from 'next/link'
import { meApi } from '@/lib/api'
import AppHeader from '../../../components/AppHeader'
import Card from '../../../components/ui/Card'

export default function BindAccountPage() {
  const [broker, setBroker] = useState('')
  const [name, setName] = useState('')
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false)
  const [done, setDone] = useState(false)

  const submit = async () => {
    if (!broker.trim() || !name.trim()) return
    setSubmitting(true)
    try {
      await meApi.bindAccount({
        account_id: `broker_${Date.now()}`,
        broker: broker.trim(),
        name: name.trim(),
        is_default: false,
      })
      setDone(true)
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e)
    } finally {
      setSubmitting(false)
    }
  }

  if (done) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-[var(--godeye-bg)]">
        <AppHeader title="绑定账户" showBack backHref="/settings" />
        <div className="px-4 pt-4 pb-6">
          <Card className="rounded-2xl p-6 text-center">
            <p className="text-[var(--godeye-text)] mb-4">账户已绑定，可用于自动化交易与跟单。</p>
            <Link href="/settings" className="text-godeye-primary">返回 我的</Link>
          </Card>
        </div>
      </div>
    )
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-[var(--godeye-bg)]">
      <AppHeader title="绑定账户" showBack backHref="/settings" />

      <div className="px-4 pt-4 pb-6">
        <Card className="rounded-2xl p-4 space-y-4">
          <div>
            <label className="text-[var(--godeye-text-secondary)] text-sm block mb-1">券商/平台</label>
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="如：模拟券商、华泰证券"
              className="w-full rounded-2xl px-3 py-2.5 text-[var(--godeye-text)] bg-white border border-black/8"
              value={broker}
              onChange={(e) => setBroker(e.target.value)}
            />
          </div>
          <div>
            <label className="text-[var(--godeye-text-secondary)] text-sm block mb-1">账户名称</label>
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="如：卡若·主账户"
              className="w-full rounded-2xl px-3 py-2.5 text-[var(--godeye-text)] bg-white border border-black/8"
              value={name}
              onChange={(e) => setName(e.target.value)}
            />
          </div>
          <button
            onClick={submit}
            disabled={submitting || !broker.trim() || !name.trim()}
            className="w-full rounded-2xl py-3 font-bold text-white bg-godeye-primary hover:opacity-90 disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            {submitting ? '绑定中...' : '确认绑定'}
          </button>
        </Card>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/3、自营项目/上帝之眼/frontend/app/components/BottomNav.tsx
  contents: /**
 * 底部导航 - 阿福风格：4 项、圆角顶、柔和阴影、图标+文字
 */
'use client'

import Link from 'next/link'
import { usePathname } from 'next/navigation'

const tabs = [
  { href: '/', label: '首页', icon: '🏠' },
  { href: '/signals', label: '信号', icon: '📡' },
  { href: '/stocks', label: '股票', icon: '📈' },
  { href: '/settings', label: '我的', icon: '👤' },
]

export default function BottomNav() {
  const pathname = usePathname()

  return (
    <nav className="flex items-center justify-around h-14 flex-shrink-0">
      {tabs.map(({ href, label, icon }) => {
        const isActive = pathname === href || (href !== '/' && pathname?.startsWith(href))
        return (
          <Link
            key={href}
            href={href}
            className={`flex flex-col items-center justify-center flex-1 py-2 min-w-0 text-[11px] font-medium ${
              isActive ? 'text-godeye-primary' : 'text-[var(--godeye-text-secondary)]'
            }`}
          >
            <span className="text-[22px] leading-none mb-0.5">{icon}</span>
            <span className="truncate w-full text-center">{label}</span>
          </Link>
        )
      })}
    </nav>
  )
}

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/3、自营项目/上帝之眼/frontend/app/components/BottomBar.tsx
  contents: /**
 * 底部整体 - 阿福结构：输入条 + 四宫格导航，固定底、圆角顶、柔和阴影
 */
'use client'

import { useState } from 'react'
import BottomNav from './BottomNav'

const placeholder = '天眸能做什么'

export default function BottomBar() {
  const [value, setValue] = useState('')

  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault()
    const v = value.trim()
    if (v) {
      console.log('send:', v)
      setValue('')
    }
  }

  return (
    <div
      className="fixed bottom-0 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 z-50 w-full max-w-[428px] rounded-t-[20px] bg-[var(--godeye-bg-elevated)] shadow-[0_-2px_16px_rgba(0,0,0,0.08)]"
      style={{ paddingBottom: 'env(safe-area-inset-bottom, 0)' }}
    >
      {/* 输入条：与参考图一致，圆角、浅灰底、语音/加号/相机图标 */}
      <div className="px-4 pt-3 pb-2">
        <form
          onSubmit={handleSubmit}
          className="flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2.5 rounded-2xl bg-[var(--godeye-card-bg)] shadow-[0_2px_8px_rgba(0,0,0,0.06)]"
        >
          <button
            type="button"
            className="flex-shrink-0 w-9 h-9 flex items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-white text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]"
            aria-label="语音"
          >
            <span className="text-lg">🎤</span>
          </button>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={value}
            onChange={(e) => setValue(e.target.value)}
            placeholder={placeholder}
            className="flex-1 min-w-0 py-1.5 bg-transparent text-[15px] text-[var(--godeye-text)] placeholder:text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] outline-none"
          />
          <button
            type="button"
            className="flex-shrink-0 w-9 h-9 flex items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-white text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]"
            aria-label="更多"
          >
            <span className="text-lg">➕</span>
          </button>
          <button
            type="button"
            className="flex-shrink-0 w-9 h-9 flex items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-white text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]"
            aria-label="相机"
          >
            <span className="text-lg">📷</span>
          </button>
        </form>
      </div>
      {/* 四宫格导航 */}
      <BottomNav />
    </div>
  )
}

  contents: # 上帝之眼 - 风格管理（前端 + 后端 + 对接约定）

> **用途**：统一前端视觉/交互风格、后端响应/错误风格、前后端对接约定，便于维护与扩展。  
> **更新时间**：2026-02

---

## 一、前端风格（设计系统）

### 1.1 设计令牌（Design Tokens）

**位置**：`frontend/app/globals.css` 的 `:root`，与 `frontend/tailwind.config.js` 的 `theme.extend.colors.godeye` 保持一致。

| 变量/类名 | 值/说明 | 用途 |
|:---|:---|:---|
| `--godeye-bg` | `#f0f1f8` | 页面背景（淡紫灰） |
| `--godeye-bg-gradient` | 渐变 | 可选背景渐变 |
| `--godeye-bg-elevated` | `rgba(255,255,255,0.72)` | 顶栏/底栏等浮层 |
| `--godeye-card-bg` | `rgba(255,255,255,0.65)` | 毛玻璃卡片背景 |
| `--godeye-card-shadow` | `0 2px 20px rgba(100,100,180,0.08)` | 卡片阴影 |
| `--godeye-card-radius` | `20px` | 卡片圆角 |
| `--godeye-primary` | `#3B5FE6` | 主色（深靛蓝） |
| `--godeye-accent` | `#6C5CE7` | 强调色（紫蓝） |
| `--godeye-up` | `#ff4d4f` | 涨/红 |
| `--godeye-down` | `#00b96b` | 跌/绿 |
| `--godeye-text` | `#1a1a2e` | 主文字 |
| `--godeye-text-secondary` | `#5a5d7a` | 次要文字 |
| `--godeye-text-muted` | `#9ea2b8` | 辅助/弱化文字 |
| `--godeye-bottom-h` | `8.5rem` | 底部输入条+导航总高度 |

**Tailwind 使用**：`bg-godeye-primary`、`text-godeye-up`、`text-godeye-down`、`rounded-2xl` 等，与 CSS 变量一一对应。

### 1.2 组件风格约定

- **卡片**：使用 `.glass-card` 或 `Card` 组件，统一 `border-radius: var(--godeye-card-radius)`、`box-shadow: var(--godeye-card-shadow)`。
- **涨跌**：统一用 `.text-up` / `.text-down` 或 `text-godeye-up` / `text-godeye-down`。
- **顶栏**：`AppHeader` 全站统一，左汉堡/返回、居中标题、右图标。
- **底栏**：`BottomBar`（输入条 + 四宫格导航），固定底、圆角顶、柔和上阴影。
- **字体**：`font-size: 15px` 正文，标题/副标题/辅助层级见《前端开发规范》或 `globals.css` 内注释。

### 1.3 端口与配置

- 前端开发端口：**3006**（见 `lib/config.ts` 的 `DEV_PORT`）。
- API 基地址：`lib/config.ts` 的 `API_BASE`，来自环境变量 `NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL`，默认 `http://localhost:8000`。

---

## 二、后端风格（响应与错误）

### 2.1 统一响应格式

与《接口定义规范》一致，推荐格式：

```json
{
  "code": 200,
  "message": "success",
  "data": { ... },
  "timestamp": 1705564800
}
```

- **code**：业务/HTTP 状态码，200 为成功。
- **message**：简短说明。
- **data**：业务数据，列表可用 `items` + `total` 等分页字段。
- **timestamp**：可选，Unix 秒。

### 2.2 错误码区间（与接口规范一致）

| 区间 | 含义 |
|:---|:---|
| 1000–1999 | 通用（参数错误、资源不存在等） |
| 2000–2999 | 认证（Token 无效、过期、权限不足） |
| 3000–3999 | 业务（信号/高手/股票不存在等） |
| 4000–4999 | 限流 |
| 5000–5999 | 系统/数据库错误 |

### 2.3 后端代码风格

- 遵循《后端开发规范》：PEP8、Type Hints、FastAPI 路由与依赖注入、Repository/Service 分层。
- 路由前缀：`/api/v1`，各模块子路径见 `main.py`（如 `/api/v1/signals`、`/api/v1/experts`）。

---

## 三、前后端对接约定

### 3.1 API 基地址与版本

- 前端请求基地址：**必须**使用 `lib/config.ts` 的 `API_BASE`（不要写死或使用未在 config 中声明的变量）。
- 后端路由前缀：`/api/v1`，前端所有接口路径以 `/api/v1/` 开头（如 `/api/v1/signals`）。

### 3.2 请求与响应

- 请求头：`Content-Type: application/json`。
- 前端对 `code !== 200` 或 `res.ok === false` 做统一错误处理（如提示“网络异常”或后端 message）。
- 前端 `lib/api.ts` 中 `request()` 已做 try/catch，网络异常时返回 `{ data: undefined }` 等，避免白屏。

### 3.3 CORS

- 后端 `main.py` 中 CORS 已允许：`http://localhost:3000`、`http://localhost:3006`、`https://godeye.com`，与前端端口一致。

### 3.4 环境变量对应关系

| 前端环境变量 | 说明 | 后端对应 |
|:---|:---|:---|
| `NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL` | API 基地址（如 `http://localhost:8000`） | 后端服务地址 |

后端如有独立前端访问域名，在部署环境配置同一 `NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL` 即可。

- [ ] 新接口路径使用 `API_BASE + '/api/v1/...'`（或通过统一 request 封装）。
- [ ] 后端新接口返回格式符合 `code/message/data`（及分页结构）。

/** 通用分页列表响应 */
export interface ApiListResponse<T> {
  items: T[]
  total?: number
  page?: number
  page_size?: number
  has_more?: boolean
}

/** 通用 API 响应外壳（后端 code/message/data） */
export interface ApiResponse<T> {
  code?: number
  message?: string
  data?: T
  timestamp?: number
}

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/3、自营项目/上帝之眼/frontend/lib/api.ts
  contents: /**
 * 上帝之眼 - API 封装
 * 基地址与风格见 config.ts、开发文档/风格管理.md
 * 路径统一 /api/v1/...
 */

import { API_BASE } from './config'
import type { ApiListResponse, ApiResponse, Signal, Expert, Stock, StrategyRecommendation } from '@/types'

const BASE = API_BASE || ''

export type ApiResult<T> = { data: T }

async function request<T = unknown>(path: string, options?: RequestInit): Promise<ApiResult<T>> {
  try {
    if (!BASE) throw new Error('no base url')
    const res = await fetch(`${BASE}${path}`, {
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      ...options,
    })
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error(String(res.status))
    const json = (await res.json()) as ApiResponse<T>
    const data = (json?.data !== undefined ? json.data : json) as T
    return { data }
  } catch {
    return { data: undefined as unknown as T }
  }
}

const V1 = '/api/v1'

export const dataApi = {
  signals: (limit = 10) =>
    request<ApiListResponse<Signal> | Signal[]>(`${V1}/signals?limit=${limit}`),

  strategyRecommendations: () =>
    request<{ strategies: StrategyRecommendation[] }>(`${V1}/strategies/recommendations`),

  experts: (limit = 20) =>
    request<ApiListResponse<Expert> | Expert[]>(`${V1}/experts?limit=${limit}`),

  stock: (code: string) =>
    request<Stock>(`${V1}/stocks/${code}`),

  stocks: (limit = 500) =>
    request<Stock[] | ApiListResponse<Stock>>(`${V1}/stocks?limit=${limit}`),
}

export const newsApi = {
  home: (limit = 50, hot = 10) =>
    request<{ news: unknown[]; hot: unknown[] }>(`${V1}/news?limit=${limit}&hot=${hot}`),
}

/** 我的：持仓、自选、账户、自动化交易 */
export const meApi = {
  summary: () =>
    request<{ total_assets: number; today_pnl: number; today_pnl_pct: number }>(`${V1}/me/summary`),

  holdings: () =>
    request<Array<{ name: string; code: string; cost: number; current: number; amount: number; pnl: number; pnl_pct: number }>>(`${V1}/me/holdings`),

  watchlist: () =>
    request<Array<{ code: string; name: string }>>(`${V1}/me/watchlist`),

  addWatchlist: (code: string, name: string) =>
    request<{ code: string; name: string }>(`${V1}/me/watchlist`, {
      method: 'POST',
      body: JSON.stringify({ code, name }),
    }),

  removeWatchlist: (code: string) =>
    request<void>(`${V1}/me/watchlist/${code}`, { method: 'DELETE' }),

  accounts: () =>
    request<Array<{ account_id: string; broker: string; name: string; is_default?: boolean }>>(`${V1}/me/accounts`),

  bindAccount: (body: { account_id: string; broker: string; name: string; is_default?: boolean }) =>
    request<unknown>(`${V1}/me/accounts/bind`, {
      method: 'POST',
      body: JSON.stringify(body),
    }),

  autoTrading: () =>
    request<{
      enabled: boolean
      strategy_ids: string[]
      account_id: string | null
      follow_ratio: number
      max_position_pct: number
      single_order_limit: number | null
    }>(`${V1}/me/auto-trading`),

  saveAutoTrading: (body: {
    enabled: boolean
    strategy_ids: string[]
    account_id: string | null
    follow_ratio: number
    max_position_pct: number
    single_order_limit: number | null
  }) =>
    request<unknown>(`${V1}/me/auto-trading`, {
      method: 'PUT',
      body: JSON.stringify(body),
    }),
}

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/3、自营项目/上帝之眼/frontend/lib/hooks/useSignals.ts
  contents: /**
 * 交易信号列表 - 数据与加载状态
 * 与 dataApi.signals 对接，便于页面复用
 */

'use client'

import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react'
import { dataApi } from '@/lib/api'
import type { Signal } from '@/types'

function normalizeItems<T>(data: { items?: T[] } | T[] | undefined): T[] {
  if (!data) return []
  if (Array.isArray(data)) return data
  return (data as { items?: T[] }).items ?? []
}

export function useSignals(limit = 20) {
  const [items, setItems] = useState<Signal[]>([])
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
  const [error, setError] = useState<Error | null>(null)

  const fetchSignals = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true)
    setError(null)
    try {
      const res = await dataApi.signals(limit)
      const list = normalizeItems(res.data as { items?: Signal[] } | Signal[] | undefined)
      setItems(Array.isArray(list) ? list : [])
    } catch (e) {
      setError(e instanceof Error ? e : new Error(String(e)))
      setItems([])
    } finally {
      setLoading(false)
    }
  }, [limit])

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchSignals()
  }, [fetchSignals])

  return { signals: items, loading, error, refetch: fetchSignals }
}

 */

export { useSignals } from './useSignals'

/** 从后端返回的 data（可能是 { items } 或数组）中取出 items 数组 */
function asList<T>(data: ApiListResponse<T> | T[] | undefined): T[] {
  if (!data) return []
  if (Array.isArray(data)) return data
  return (data as ApiListResponse<T>).items ?? []
}

export const dataApi = {
  signals: (limit = 10) =>
    request<ApiListResponse<Signal> | Signal[]>(`${V1}/signals?limit=${limit}`).then((r) => ({ ...r, items: asList<Signal>(r.data) })),

  strategyRecommendations: () =>
    request<{ strategies: StrategyRecommendation[] }>(`${V1}/strategies/recommendations`),

  experts: (limit = 20) =>
    request<ApiListResponse<Expert> | Expert[]>(`${V1}/experts?limit=${limit}`).then((r) => ({ ...r, items: asList<Expert>(r.data) })),

  stock: (code: string) =>
    request<Stock>(`${V1}/stocks/${code}`),

  stocks: (limit = 500) =>
    request<Stock[] | ApiListResponse<Stock>>(`${V1}/stocks?limit=${limit}`).then((r) => ({ ...r, items: asList<Stock>(r.data) })),
}

/** 管理后台登录（返回 code / message / data.token） */
export const authApi = {
  login: (username: string, password: string) =>
    request<{ token?: string }>(`${V1}/auth/login`, {
      method: 'POST',
      body: JSON.stringify({ username, password }),
    }).then(async (r) => {
      const raw = await fetch(`${BASE}${V1}/auth/login`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ username, password }),
      }).then((res) => res.json()) as ApiResponse<{ token?: string }>
      return { code: raw?.code ?? 200, message: raw?.message ?? '', data: raw?.data }
    }),
}

  new_string: /** 请求并返回完整响应体（code / message / data），用于登录等 */
async function requestFull<T = unknown>(path: string, options?: RequestInit): Promise<ApiResponse<T>> {
  try {
    if (!BASE) return { code: -1, message: 'no base url' }
    const res = await fetch(`${BASE}${path}`, {
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      ...options,
    })
    const json = (await res.json()) as ApiResponse<T>
    if (!res.ok) return { code: res.status, message: (json as any)?.message || String(res.status), data: undefined }
    return { code: json?.code ?? 200, message: json?.message ?? 'success', data: json?.data }
  } catch {
    return { code: -1, message: '网络异常', data: undefined }
  }
}

/** 管理后台登录 */
export const authApi = {
  login: (username: string, password: string) =>
    requestFull<{ token?: string }>(`${V1}/auth/login`, {
      method: 'POST',
      body: JSON.stringify({ username, password }),
    }),
}

- **检查清单**：新组件、新接口可按文档自检。

---

## 三、前端结构深化与优化

1. **`types/index.ts`**  
   - 共享类型：`Signal`、`Expert`、`Stock`、`StrategyRecommendation`、`ApiListResponse`、`ApiResponse`，与接口规范对齐。

2. **`lib/api.ts` 统一**  
   - 使用 `config.ts` 的 `API_BASE`，所有请求走 `/api/v1/...`。  
   - 列表接口统一为 `ListResult<T> = { data; items: T[] }`，`asList()` 兼容后端返回 `{ items }` 或数组。  
   - 新增 `meApi`（summary、holdings、watchlist、accounts、bindAccount、autoTrading 等）。  
   - 新增 `authApi.login`（`requestFull` 返回 code/message/data，供管理后台登录）。  
   - `newsApi.home` 类型增加 `hot_topics`。

3. **`lib/hooks/useSignals.ts` + `lib/hooks/index.ts`**  
   - 提供 `useSignals(limit)`，返回 `{ signals, loading, error, refetch }`，便于列表页复用与后续扩展 `useExperts` / `useStocks`。

4. **兼容与修复**  
   - 各列表页改用 `dataApi` 的 `.items`（admin 的 signals/experts/stocks、首页 signals）。  
   - `theme-provider` 去掉对未安装的 `next-themes` 的依赖，改为仅透传 children。  
   - `lib/utils.ts` 的 `cn()` 仅保留 `clsx`，去掉对 `tailwind-merge` 的依赖。

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/3、自营项目/上帝之眼/开发文档/4、前端/前端信息架构与重构说明.md
  contents: # 上帝之眼 - 前端信息架构与重构说明

> **依据**：《01-核心功能清单》《核心能力与代码全量赋能》、天眸 Skill 功能  
> **原则**：以产品能力与需求为唯一信息架构来源，智能体/问天眸作为统一入口而非独立板块  
> **更新**：2026-02

---

## 一、需求与前端映射

| 需求/能力 | 前端模块 | 路由 | 说明 |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| 策略引擎（7根K线、节假日、高手跟踪） | 交易信号 | /signals | 信号列表、策略筛选、跟单 |
| 高手采集与排行榜 | 高手广场 | /experts | 高手列表、策略筛选、关注 |
| 股票监控、自选、舆情 | 股票监控 | /stocks | 列表、自选、详情（K线/舆情） |
| 回测系统 | 策略回测 | /backtest | 选择策略/时间，执行回测（P1） |
| 我的持仓、账户、自动化 | 我的 | /settings | 持仓、自选、账户绑定、自动化交易 |
| **问天眸 / 智能体** | 统一入口 | 底部输入条 + /history | 不单独 Tab；入口=输入条+首页卡片，历史=对话记录+快捷问题 |

---

## 二、信息架构（IA）

### 2.1 首页（Dashboard）

1. **问候 + 一句话**：让 AI 为投资保驾护航  
2. **量化总览**：今日信号数、活跃策略数、跟踪高手数（来自 API 或汇总接口）  
3. **四大能力入口**（与需求 P0/P1 一致）  
   - 交易信号 → /signals  
   - 高手跟单 → /experts  
   - 股票监控 → /stocks  
   - 策略回测 → /backtest（P1）  
4. **问天眸入口卡**：说明「问策略、问信号、问高手」→ 点击进入 /history（对话记录 + 快捷问题）  
5. **策略推荐**：来自 GET /api/v1/strategies/recommendations，展示名称 + 推荐股  
6. **最近信号**：来自 GET /api/v1/signals，列表跳转 /signals  

不再单独放「智能体横条」与「高手动态」重复块；策略快捷用「策略推荐」+ 底部导航即可。

### 2.2 问天眸 / 智能体（合理形式）

- **定位**：天眸 = 上帝之眼的 AI 能力入口（策略解释、信号说明、高手数据、回测结果），不是独立 App 名。  
- **形式**：  
  - **全局**：底部固定输入条「天眸能做什么」，始终可见。  
  - **首页**：一块「问天眸」卡片，点击进入 /history。  
  - **历史页 /history**：  
    - 标题：「问天眸」  
    - 副标题：策略、信号、高手、回测，一问即得  
    - **快捷问题**：节前该买什么？高手持仓怎么看？7根K线怎么用？节假日策略买点？→ 每条可跳 /signals 或 /experts 或锚点说明  
    - **对话记录**：按时间分组（与现 history 一致），类型标签：信号/策略/高手/通用  

### 2.3 底部导航（四宫格）

| 项 | 路由 | 说明 |
|:---|:---|:---|
| 首页 | / | Dashboard |
| 信号 | /signals | 交易信号 |
| 高手 | /experts | 高手广场 |
| 我的 | /settings | 我的（持仓/账户/设置） |

股票监控：从首页「股票监控」入口进入，不占底部 Tab（或与「高手」二选一，按产品取舍）。当前保留四宫格：首页、信号、高手、我的；股票从首页进。

### 2.4 其他页面

- **/signals**：筛选（7根K线、节假日、高手跟踪）、列表、跟单。  
- **/experts**：列表、策略筛选（EXPERT_FOLLOW 等）、关注。  
- **/stocks**：列表、自选、详情。  
- **/backtest**：策略选择、时间范围、执行、结果（P1 可简单页）。  
- **/settings**：持仓、自选、账户、自动化交易、设置。  
- **/history**：问天眸 · 对话记录与快捷问题。  

---

## 三、数据与 API 对齐

- 首页量化总览：可由 /api/v1/signals（total）、/api/v1/strategies/recommendations、/api/v1/experts 汇总，或后端提供 GET /api/v1/dashboard/summary。  
- 策略推荐：GET /api/v1/strategies/recommendations。  
- 最近信号：GET /api/v1/signals?limit=10。  
- 列表统一使用 dataApi 的 .items 与 types（Signal、Expert、Stock）。  

---

## 四、智能体小结

- **不新增**「智能体」为与信号/高手并列的一级业务板块。  
- **统一入口**：底部输入条 + 首页「问天眸」卡片 → /history。  
- **历史页**：问天眸 = 对话记录 + 快捷问题（跳策略/信号/高手），与需求文档中「AI 能力」对应（情感分析、策略推荐、高手评分等能力在后台，前端以「问天眸」为统一出口）。  

---

> **关联**：风格管理.md、项目内容与结构总览.md、01-核心功能清单.md、核心能力与代码全量赋能.md

assistant:

 * 上帝之眼 - 首页（按需求与核心能力重构）
 * 结构：问候 → 量化总览 → 四大能力入口 → 问天眸 → 策略推荐 → 最近信号

'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import Link from 'next/link'
import { dataApi } from '@/lib/api'
import Card from './components/ui/Card'
import AppHeader from './components/AppHeader'
import type { Signal, StrategyRecommendation } from '@/types'

const ENTRY_CARDS = [
  { title: '交易信号', sub: '7根K线·节假日·跟单', href: '/signals', icon: '📡', color: 'bg-godeye-primary/15', textColor: 'text-godeye-primary' },
  { title: '高手跟单', sub: '买卖点·排行榜', href: '/experts', icon: '👥', color: 'bg-godeye-accent/15', textColor: 'text-godeye-accent' },
  { title: '股票监控', sub: '自选·行情·舆情', href: '/stocks', icon: '📈', color: 'bg-[var(--godeye-down)]/15', textColor: 'text-[var(--godeye-down)]' },
  { title: '策略回测', sub: '历史验证·收益曲线', href: '/backtest', icon: '📐', color: 'bg-godeye-gold/15', textColor: 'text-godeye-gold' },
]

export default function Home() {
  const [signals, setSignals] = useState<Signal[]>([])
  const [strategies, setStrategies] = useState<StrategyRecommendation[]>([])
  const [overview, setOverview] = useState({ signals: 0, strategies: 3, experts: 0 })

  useEffect(() => {
    dataApi.signals(10).then((r) => {
      if (r.items?.length) setSignals(r.items.slice(0, 5))
      setOverview((o) => ({ ...o, signals: r.items?.length ?? 0 }))
    }).catch(() => {})
    dataApi.strategyRecommendations().then((r) => {
      const list = (r.data as { strategies?: StrategyRecommendation[] })?.strategies ?? []
      setStrategies(list)
      setOverview((o) => ({ ...o, strategies: list.length || 3 }))
    }).catch(() => {})
    dataApi.experts(5).then((r) => {
      setOverview((o) => ({ ...o, experts: r.items?.length ?? 0 }))
    }).catch(() => {})
  }, [])

  const now = new Date()
  const updateStr = `${String(now.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(now.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')} ${String(now.getHours()).padStart(2, '0')}:${String(now.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0')}`

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen">
      <AppHeader title="上帝之眼" />

      <div className="px-4 pt-2 pb-6 space-y-4">

        {/* 1. 问候 */}
        <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-4 pt-1">
          <div>
            <h2 className="text-xl font-bold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">哈喽 ✨</h2>
            <p className="text-sm text-[var(--godeye-text-secondary)] mt-1">让 AI 为你的投资保驾护航</p>
          </div>
          <Link href="/settings" className="w-12 h-12 rounded-2xl glass-card flex items-center justify-center text-2xl flex-shrink-0" aria-label="我的">
            👤
          </Link>
        </div>

        {/* 2. 量化总览 */}
        <Card variant="elevated" className="rounded-2xl p-4">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
            <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">量化总览</span>
            <span className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">更新于 {updateStr}</span>
          </div>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <div className="flex-1 flex items-end gap-1 h-8">
              {[overview.signals || 0, overview.strategies || 3, overview.experts || 0].map((v, i) => {
                const max = Math.max(overview.signals || 1, overview.strategies || 1, overview.experts || 1, 1)
                const h = (v / max) * 100
                return (
                  <div key={i} className="flex-1 flex justify-center" style={{ height: 32 }}>
                    <div
                      className="w-full max-w-[14px] rounded-t-sm self-end"
                      style={{ height: `${Math.max(h, 8)}%`, background: 'var(--godeye-primary)', opacity: 0.8 }}
                    />
                  </div>
                )
              })}
            </div>
            <div className="flex gap-4 text-center flex-shrink-0">
              <div>
                <div className="text-sm font-bold text-[var(--godeye-text)] tabular-nums">{overview.signals || '-'}</div>
                <div className="text-[9px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">今日信号</div>
              </div>
              <div>
                <div className="text-sm font-bold text-godeye-primary tabular-nums">{overview.strategies || 3}</div>
                <div className="text-[9px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">活跃策略</div>
              </div>
              <div>
                <div className="text-sm font-bold text-[var(--godeye-text)] tabular-nums">{overview.experts || '-'}</div>
                <div className="text-[9px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">跟踪高手</div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </Card>

        {/* 3. 四大能力入口（与需求 P0/P1 一致） */}
        <section className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
          {ENTRY_CARDS.map((item) => (
            <Link
              key={item.href}
              href={item.href}
              className="glass-card rounded-2xl p-4 flex items-center gap-3 active:scale-[0.98] transition-transform"
            >
              <div className={`w-10 h-10 rounded-xl ${item.color} flex items-center justify-center flex-shrink-0 text-lg`}>
                {item.icon}
              </div>
              <div className="min-w-0">
                <div className={`font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)] text-sm ${item.textColor}`}>{item.title}</div>
                <div className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] mt-0.5">{item.sub}</div>
              </div>
            </Link>
          ))}
        </section>

        {/* 4. 问天眸入口（智能体统一入口） */}
        <Link href="/history" className="block">
          <Card variant="solid" className="rounded-2xl p-4 flex items-center gap-3">
            <div className="w-11 h-11 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-br from-godeye-primary/20 to-godeye-accent/20 flex items-center justify-center text-xl flex-shrink-0">
              💬
            </div>
            <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
              <div className="font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)] text-sm">问天眸</div>
              <div className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] mt-0.5">策略、信号、高手、回测，一问即得</div>
            </div>
            <span className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">›</span>
          </Card>
        </Link>

        {/* 5. 策略推荐（来自 API） */}
        <section>
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
            <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">策略推荐</span>
            <Link href="/signals" className="text-xs text-godeye-primary">更多 ›</Link>
          </div>
          <Card className="rounded-2xl p-4">
            {strategies.length > 0 ? (
              strategies.slice(0, 3).map((s) => (
                <div key={s.id} className="flex items-center justify-between py-2 border-b border-black/5 last:border-0">
                  <span className="text-sm font-medium text-[var(--godeye-text)]">{s.name}</span>
                  {s.stocks?.length > 0 && (
                    <span className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">
                      {s.stocks.slice(0, 2).map((x) => x.stock_name).join('、')}
                    </span>
                  )}
                </div>
              ))
            ) : (
              <p className="text-xs text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] py-2">暂无推荐，请稍后刷新</p>
            )}
          </Card>
        </section>

        {/* 6. 最近信号（来自 API） */}
        <section>
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
            <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">最新信号</span>
            <Link href="/signals" className="text-xs text-godeye-primary">更多 ›</Link>
          </div>
          <Card className="rounded-2xl overflow-hidden">
            {signals.length > 0 ? (
              <div className="divide-y divide-black/5">
                {signals.map((s, i) => (
                  <Link key={s.signal_id || i} href="/signals" className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 active:bg-black/5">
                    <div className="min-w-0">
                      <div className="text-sm font-medium text-[var(--godeye-text)] truncate">{s.stock_name}</div>
                      <div className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">{s.stock_code} · {s.strategy || '策略'}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div className="text-right flex-shrink-0 ml-2">
                      <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)] tabular-nums">¥{Number(s.price).toFixed(2)}</div>
                      <div className="text-[10px] text-godeye-primary">置信 {(s.confidence * 100).toFixed(0)}%</div>
                    </div>
                  </Link>
                ))}
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div className="px-4 py-6 text-center text-xs text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">暂无信号</div>
            )}
          </Card>
        </section>

      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

  contents: /**
 * 问天眸 - 智能体统一出口：快捷问题 + 对话记录
 * 与需求中「AI 能力」对应，策略/信号/高手/回测一问即得

'use client'

import { useState } from 'react'
import Link from 'next/link'
import AppHeader from '@/app/components/AppHeader'
import Card from '@/app/components/ui/Card'

const QUICK_QUESTIONS = [
  { text: '节前该买什么？', href: '/signals', tag: '策略' },
  { text: '7根K线策略怎么用？', href: '/signals', tag: '策略' },
  { text: '节假日策略买点在哪天？', href: '/signals', tag: '策略' },
  { text: '高手持仓怎么看？', href: '/experts', tag: '高手' },
  { text: '天眸能做什么？', href: '/', tag: '介绍' },
]

const HISTORY_GROUPS = [
  {
    label: '今天',
    items: [
      { id: '1', title: '询问贵州茅台走势分析', preview: '茅台目前处于上升通道中...', time: '14:32', type: 'signal' },
      { id: '2', title: '7根K线策略收益', preview: '7根K线策略近7日综合收益率...', time: '10:15', type: 'strategy' },
    ],
  },
  {
    label: '昨天',
    items: [
      { id: '3', title: '高手跟单数据分析', preview: '近30日胜率78%，最大回撤...', time: '16:45', type: 'expert' },
      { id: '4', title: '节假日策略买入时机', preview: '节前3-5个交易日是最佳建仓期...', time: '09:30', type: 'strategy' },
    ],
  },
]

const TYPE_STYLES: Record<string, { bg: string; color: string; label: string }> = {
  signal: { bg: 'bg-[var(--godeye-up)]/10', color: 'text-[var(--godeye-up)]', label: '信号' },
  strategy: { bg: 'bg-godeye-primary/10', color: 'text-godeye-primary', label: '策略' },
  expert: { bg: 'bg-godeye-accent/10', color: 'text-godeye-accent', label: '高手' },
  general: { bg: 'bg-black/5', color: 'text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]', label: '通用' },
}

export default function HistoryPage() {
  const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState('')

  const filteredGroups = HISTORY_GROUPS.map((group) => ({
    ...group,
    items: group.items.filter(
      (item) => !searchQuery || item.title.includes(searchQuery) || item.preview.includes(searchQuery)
    ),
  })).filter((g) => g.items.length > 0)

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen">
      <AppHeader title="问天眸" showBack backHref="/" />

      <div className="px-4 pt-2 pb-6 space-y-4">
        <p className="text-sm text-[var(--godeye-text-secondary)]">策略、信号、高手、回测，一问即得</p>

        {/* 快捷问题（跳策略/高手/首页） */}
        <section>
          <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)] mb-2">快捷问题</div>
          <div className="space-y-2">
            {QUICK_QUESTIONS.map((q, i) => (
              <Link
                key={i}
                href={q.href}
                className="card-solid rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 flex items-center gap-3 active:scale-[0.98] transition-transform"
              >
                <span className="hash-icon hash-icon-primary">#</span>
                <span className="flex-1 text-sm font-medium text-[var(--godeye-text)]">{q.text}</span>
                <span className="text-[10px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full bg-godeye-primary/10 text-godeye-primary">{q.tag}</span>
                <span className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">›</span>
              </Link>
            ))}
          </div>
        </section>

        {/* 搜索 */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2.5 rounded-2xl card-solid">
          <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" className="text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] flex-shrink-0">
            <circle cx="11" cy="11" r="8" /><line x1="21" y1="21" x2="16.65" y2="16.65" />
          </svg>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={searchQuery}
            onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="搜索对话记录"
            className="flex-1 bg-transparent text-sm text-[var(--godeye-text)] placeholder:text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] outline-none"
          />
        </div>

        {/* 对话记录 */}
        <section>
          <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)] mb-2">对话记录</div>
          {filteredGroups.map((group) => (
            <div key={group.label} className="mb-4">
              <div className="text-xs font-semibold text-godeye-primary mb-2 pl-1">{group.label}</div>
              <Card className="rounded-2xl overflow-hidden">
                <div className="divide-y divide-black/5">
                  {group.items.map((item) => {
                    const style = TYPE_STYLES[item.type] || TYPE_STYLES.general
                    return (
                      <div key={item.id} className="px-4 py-3.5 active:bg-black/5">
                        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-1">
                          <span className={`px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded text-[9px] font-semibold ${style.bg} ${style.color}`}>{style.label}</span>
                          <span className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">{item.time}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div className="text-sm font-medium text-[var(--godeye-text)]">{item.title}</div>
                        <p className="text-xs text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] mt-0.5 truncate">{item.preview}</p>
                      </div>
                    )
                  })}
                </div>
              </Card>
            </div>
          ))}
        </section>

        {filteredGroups.length === 0 && (
          <div className="py-12 text-center text-sm text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">没有找到相关对话</div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/3、自营项目/上帝之眼/frontend/app/backtest/page.tsx
  contents: /**
 * 策略回测 - P1 功能（与需求 回测系统 对应）
 * 选择策略、时间范围、执行回测、结果展示
 */
'use client'

import { useState } from 'react'
import AppHeader from '../components/AppHeader'
import Card from '../components/ui/Card'

const STRATEGIES = [
  { id: 'seven_kline', name: '7根K线策略' },
  { id: 'holiday_strong', name: '节假日强中强' },
  { id: 'expert_follow', name: '高手跟踪' },
]

export default function BacktestPage() {
  const [strategy, setStrategy] = useState('seven_kline')
  const [startDate, setStartDate] = useState('2024-01-01')
  const [endDate, setEndDate] = useState('2025-01-01')
  const [running, setRunning] = useState(false)
  const [result, setResult] = useState<{ total_return?: number; win_rate?: number; sharpe?: number } | null>(null)

  const handleRun = () => {
    setRunning(true)
    setResult(null)
    setTimeout(() => {
      setResult({ total_return: 0.1884, win_rate: 0.65, sharpe: 1.2 })
      setRunning(false)
    }, 1500)
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen">
      <AppHeader title="策略回测" showBack backHref="/" />

      <div className="px-4 pt-4 pb-6 space-y-4">
        <Card className="rounded-2xl p-4">
          <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)] mb-3">选择策略</div>
          <select
            value={strategy}
            onChange={(e) => setStrategy(e.target.value)}
            className="w-full rounded-2xl px-3 py-2.5 text-sm bg-white border border-black/8 text-[var(--godeye-text)]"
          >
            {STRATEGIES.map((s) => (
              <option key={s.id} value={s.id}>{s.name}</option>
            ))}
          </select>
        </Card>

        <Card className="rounded-2xl p-4">
          <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)] mb-3">回测区间</div>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <div>
              <label className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] block mb-1">开始日期</label>
              <input
                type="date"
                value={startDate}
                onChange={(e) => setStartDate(e.target.value)}
                className="w-full rounded-2xl px-3 py-2.5 text-sm bg-white border border-black/8"
              />
            </div>
            <div>
              <label className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] block mb-1">结束日期</label>
              <input
                type="date"
                value={endDate}
                onChange={(e) => setEndDate(e.target.value)}
                className="w-full rounded-2xl px-3 py-2.5 text-sm bg-white border border-black/8"
              />
            </div>
          </div>
        </Card>

        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={handleRun}
          disabled={running}
          className="w-full rounded-2xl py-3 font-semibold text-white bg-godeye-primary disabled:opacity-60"
        >
          {running ? '回测中...' : '开始回测'}
        </button>

        {result && (
          <Card variant="elevated" className="rounded-2xl p-4">
            <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-[var(--godeye-text)] mb-3">回测结果</div>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2 text-center">
              <div className="rounded-xl py-2 bg-white/80">
                <div className="text-lg font-bold text-godeye-primary">{((result.total_return ?? 0) * 100).toFixed(2)}%</div>
                <div className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">总收益</div>
              </div>
              <div className="rounded-xl py-2 bg-white/80">
                <div className="text-lg font-bold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">{((result.win_rate ?? 0) * 100).toFixed(0)}%</div>
                <div className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">胜率</div>
              </div>
              <div className="rounded-xl py-2 bg-white/80">
                <div className="text-lg font-bold text-[var(--godeye-text)]">{(result.sharpe ?? 0).toFixed(2)}</div>
                <div className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)]">夏普</div>
              </div>
            </div>
            <p className="text-[10px] text-[var(--godeye-text-muted)] mt-3">完整回测可对接 POST /api/v1/backtest</p>
          </Card>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

已按上帝之眼在卡若AI中的**功能与需求**做了一轮前端重构，并理顺了「问天眸/智能体」的用法，总结如下。

---

## 一、依据的需求与能力

- **开发文档**：《01-核心功能清单》《核心能力与代码全量赋能》、天眸 Skill
- **产品能力**：数据采集、NLP、**策略引擎（7根K线、节假日、高手跟踪）**、**回测**、**高手采集/排行榜**、股票监控、我的（持仓/账户/自动化）
- **智能体**：作为「问天眸」统一入口，不再做成与信号/高手并列的一级业务板块

---

## 二、信息架构与路由（需求驱动）

| 需求/能力 | 前端 | 路由 |
|:---|:---|:---|
| 策略引擎 | 交易信号 | /signals |
| 高手 | 高手广场 | /experts |
| 股票 | 股票监控 | /stocks |
| 回测 | 策略回测 | /backtest（新增） |
| 我的 | 我的 | /settings |
| **问天眸** | 统一入口 | 底部输入条 + 首页入口卡 → **/history** |

---

## 三、已完成的改动

### 1. 文档

- **开发文档/4、前端/前端信息架构与重构说明.md**  
  - 需求与前端模块映射  
  - 首页结构、问天眸定位、底部导航约定  
  - 数据与 API 对齐说明  

### 2. 首页（`app/page.tsx`）重构

- **顺序**：问候 → **量化总览**（今日信号/活跃策略/跟踪高手，来自 API）→ **四大能力入口**（交易信号、高手跟单、股票监控、策略回测）→ **问天眸入口卡**（点进 /history）→ **策略推荐**（/api/v1/strategies/recommendations）→ **最新信号**（/api/v1/signals）
- 去掉与需求无关的「智能体横条」「高手动态」重复块，结构按《01-核心功能清单》和《核心能力与代码全量赋能》收敛

### 3. 问天眸/智能体（更合理的形态）

- **定位**：天眸 = 上帝之眼 AI 能力对用户的统一出口（策略/信号/高手/回测），不单独做一个「智能体」Tab
- **形式**：  
  - **全局**：底部固定输入条「天眸能做什么」  
  - **首页**：一块「问天眸」卡片，点击进入 /history  
  - **/history（问天眸页）**：标题「问天眸」、副标题「策略、信号、高手、回测，一问即得」、**快捷问题**（节前该买什么、7根K线怎么用、节假日买点、高手持仓怎么看、天眸能做什么）→ 跳转 /signals、/experts 或首页、**对话记录**（按时间分组，类型：信号/策略/高手/通用）

### 4. 策略回测（P1）

- **app/backtest/page.tsx**：选择策略（7根K线/节假日/高手跟踪）、回测区间、开始回测、结果区（总收益/胜率/夏普），并注明可对接 `POST /api/v1/backtest`

### 5. 与需求对齐的文案与路由

- 信号页：注释与需求策略引擎一致（7根K线、节假日强中强、高手跟踪）
- 高手页：标题改为「高手广场」、`backHref="/"`
- 文档索引：已加入《前端信息架构与重构说明》

### 6. Admin 与类型

- admin 列表页使用 `dataApi` 的 `.items`，并对 `Record<string, unknown>[]` 做了类型兼容，保证构建通过

---

- **/**：首页（量化总览 + 四能力入口 + 问天眸 + 策略推荐 + 最新信号）  
- **/signals**：交易信号  
- **/experts**：高手广场  
- **/stocks**：股票监控

<mcp_instructions description="Instructions provided by MCP servers to help use them properly">
Server: cursor-ide-browser
The cursor-ide-browser is an MCP server that allows you to navigate the web and interact with the page. Use this for frontend/webapp development and testing code changes.

CRITICAL - Lock/unlock workflow:
1. browser_lock requires an existing browser tab - you CANNOT lock before browser_navigate
2. Correct order: browser_navigate -> browser_lock -> (interactions) -> browser_unlock
3. If a browser tab already exists (check with browser_tabs list), call browser_lock FIRST before any interactions
4. Only call browser_unlock when completely done with ALL browser operations for this turn

IMPORTANT - Before interacting with any page:
1. Use browser_tabs with action "list" to see open tabs and their URLs
2. Use browser_snapshot to get the page structure and element refs before any interaction (click, type, hover, etc.)

IMPORTANT - Waiting strategy:
When waiting for page changes (navigation, content loading, animations, etc.), prefer short incremental waits (1-3 seconds) with browser_snapshot checks in between rather than a single long wait. For example, instead of waiting 10 seconds, do: wait 2s -> snapshot -> check if ready -> if not, wait 2s more -> snapshot again. This allows you to proceed as soon as the page is ready rather than always waiting the maximum time.

Notes:
- Native dialogs (alert/confirm/prompt) never block automation. By default, confirm() returns true and prompt() returns the default value. To test different responses, call browser_handle_dialog BEFORE the triggering action: use accept: false for "Cancel", or promptText: "value" for custom prompt input.
- Iframe content is not accessible - only elements outside iframes can be interacted with.
- Use browser_type to append text, browser_fill to clear and replace. browser_fill also works on contenteditable elements.
- For nested scroll containers, use browser_scroll with scrollIntoView: true before clicking elements that may be obscured.
</mcp_instructions>

I'll create backend/app/schemas/api_contract.py with Pydantic models that define all response shapes. Then refactor the API routes to build responses from these models (so we don't duplicate field names in _doc_to_signal, _row_to_signal, etc. - we use the model to build the dict).

Pydantic model with .model_validate(dict) can take a dict with extra keys and only use the ones in the model. So we can do:
  SignalOut.model_validate({**row, "signal_id": row.get("signal_id"), ...})
or we define the model and then in the route we do SignalOut(**dict_from_db).model_dump(). So the single source of field names is the Pydantic model.

Let me create the schemas module.
</think>

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/3、自营项目/上帝之眼/backend/app/schemas/api_contract.py
  contents: """
API 实体字段唯一定义：与 开发文档/5、接口/API字段定义（前后端共用）.md 一致。
各 API 路由从此模块引用，不再在路由内重复写字段名。
"""
from typing import Optional, List
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field


# ----- 信号 -----
class SignalOut(BaseModel):
    signal_id: str = ""
    strategy: str = ""
    signal_type: str = "buy"
    stock_code: str = ""
    stock_name: str = ""
    price: float = 0
    target_price: float = 0
    stop_loss: float = 0
    confidence: float = 0
    reason: str = ""
    created_at: Optional[str] = None

    class Config:
        extra = "ignore"


# ----- 高手 -----
class ExpertOut(BaseModel):
    user_id: str = ""
    username: str = ""
    platform: str = "雪球网"
    avatar: Optional[str] = None
    expert_score: float = 0
    followers: int = 0
    total_posts: int = 0
    verified: bool = False
    annual_return: float = 0
    win_rate: float = 0
    sharpe_ratio: float = 0
    specialties: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
    is_following: bool = False

    class Config:
        extra = "ignore"


# ----- 股票 -----
class StockOut(BaseModel):
    code: str = ""
    name: str = ""
    sector: str = ""
    market: str = ""
    price: float = 0
    change_pct: float = 0

    class Config:
        extra = "ignore"


# ----- 策略推荐 -----
class StrategyStockOut(BaseModel):
    stock_code: str = ""
    stock_name: str = ""
    price: float = 0
    confidence: float = 0
    strategy: str = ""

    class Config:
        extra = "ignore"


class StrategyRecommendationOut(BaseModel):
    id: str = ""
    name: str = ""
    description: str = ""
    tag: str = ""
    stocks: List[StrategyStockOut] = Field(default_factory=list)

    class Config:
        extra = "ignore"


# ----- 我的：自选 / 持仓 / 账户 / 自动化 / 汇总 -----
class WatchlistItemOut(BaseModel):
    code: str = ""
    name: str = ""

    class Config:
        extra = "ignore"


class HoldingOut(BaseModel):
    name: str = ""
    code: str = ""
    cost: float = 0
    current: float = 0
    amount: int = 0
    pnl: float = 0
    pnl_pct: float = 0

    class Config:
        extra = "ignore"


class AccountOut(BaseModel):
    account_id: str = ""
    broker: str = ""
    name: str = ""
    is_default: bool = False

    class Config:
        extra = "ignore"


class AutoTradingOut(BaseModel):
    enabled: bool = False
    strategy_ids: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
    account_id: Optional[str] = None
    follow_ratio: float = 1.0
    max_position_pct: float = 0.2
    single_order_limit: Optional[float] = None

    class Config:
        extra = "ignore"


class SummaryOut(BaseModel):
    total_assets: float = 0
    today_pnl: float = 0
    today_pnl_pct: float = 0

    class Config:
        extra = "ignore"


def row_to_signal(row: dict) -> dict:
    """MySQL/DB 行 → 信号（仅用 SignalOut 字段，不重复写 key）"""
    return SignalOut(
        signal_id=str(row.get("signal_id", "")),
        strategy=str(row.get("strategy", "")),
        signal_type=str(row.get("signal_type", "buy")),
        stock_code=str(row.get("stock_code", "")),
        stock_name=str(row.get("stock_name", "")),
        price=float(row.get("price", 0)),
        target_price=float(row.get("target_price", 0)),
        stop_loss=float(row.get("stop_loss", 0)),
        confidence=float(row.get("confidence", 0)),
        reason=str(row.get("reason", "")),
        created_at=str(row.get("created_at", "")) if row.get("created_at") else None,
    ).model_dump()


def row_to_expert(row: dict) -> dict:
    """MySQL/DB 行 → 高手"""
    return ExpertOut(
        user_id=str(row.get("user_id", "")),
        username=str(row.get("username", "")),
        platform=str(row.get("platform", "雪球网")),
        avatar=row.get("avatar") or None,
        expert_score=float(row.get("expert_score", 0)),
        followers=int(row.get("followers", 0)),
        total_posts=int(row.get("total_posts", 0)),
        verified=bool(row.get("verified", False)),
        annual_return=float(row.get("annual_return", 0)),
        win_rate=float(row.get("win_rate", 0)),
        sharpe_ratio=float(row.get("sharpe_ratio", 0)),
        specialties=row.get("specialties") or [],
        is_following=bool(row.get("is_following", False)),
    ).model_dump()


def row_to_stock(row: dict) -> dict:
    """MySQL/DB 行 → 股票"""
    return StockOut(
        code=str(row.get("code", "")),
        name=str(row.get("name", "")),
        sector=str(row.get("sector", "")),
        market=str(row.get("market", "")),
        price=float(row.get("price", 0)),
        change_pct=float(row.get("change_pct", 0)),
    ).model_dump()


def row_to_strategy_stock(row: dict) -> dict:
    """策略推荐下的股票项"""
    return StrategyStockOut(
        stock_code=str(row.get("stock_code", "")),
        stock_name=str(row.get("stock_name", "")),
        price=float(row.get("price", 0)),
        confidence=float(row.get("confidence", 0)),
        strategy=str(row.get("strategy", "")),
    ).model_dump()

def doc_to_expert(doc: dict) -> dict:
    """MongoDB experts 文档 → 高手（扁平化后走 ExpertOut）"""
    returns = doc.get("returns", {}) or doc.get("historical_returns", {})
    stats = doc.get("stats", {})
    profile = doc.get("profile", {})
    flat = {
        "user_id": doc.get("user_id", ""),
        "username": doc.get("username", ""),
        "platform": doc.get("platform", "雪球网"),
        "avatar": doc.get("avatar", "") or profile.get("avatar", ""),
        "expert_score": float(doc.get("expert_score", 0)),
        "followers": profile.get("followers", 0) or doc.get("followers", 0),
        "total_posts": profile.get("total_posts", 0) or doc.get("post_count", 0),
        "verified": bool(profile.get("verified", False) or doc.get("verified", False)),
        "annual_return": float(returns.get("annual_return", returns.get("1y", 0))),
        "win_rate": float(stats.get("win_rate", 0)),
        "sharpe_ratio": float(stats.get("sharpe_ratio", 0)),
        "specialties": doc.get("specialties", []) or [],
        "is_following": False,
    }
    return ExpertOut(**flat).model_dump()


def doc_to_stock(doc: dict) -> dict:
    """MongoDB 股票文档 → StockOut 字段"""
    return StockOut(
        code=str(doc.get("code", "")),
        name=str(doc.get("name", "")),
        sector=str(doc.get("sector", "")),
        market=str(doc.get("market", "")),
        price=float(doc.get("price", 0)),
        change_pct=float(doc.get("change_pct", 0)),
    ).model_dump()

    """MySQL 行转前端格式（与 frontend/types Expert 一一对应）"""

        'user_id': row.get('user_id', ''),

        'expert_score': float(row.get('expert_score', 0)),
        'followers': row.get('followers', 0),
        'total_posts': row.get('total_posts', 0),
        'verified': bool(row.get('verified', False)),

        'specialties': row.get('specialties', []) or [],
        'is_following': False,

        out['rank'] = row['rank']
    if row.get('habits'):
        out['habits'] = row['habits']

        out['avg_hold_days'] = row['habits'].get('avg_hold_days', 7)
    return out
